mi rigs dpe mdzod khang gi dpe tho las gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag shes bya'i gter mdzod /
... si khron mi rigs dpe skrun khang /
@# / /
bod gangs can gyi grub mtha' ris med kyi mkhas dbang brgya dang brgyad cu lhag gi gsung 'bum so so'i dkar chag phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa shes bya'i gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
stod cha mi rigs dpe mdzod khang gis bsgrigs pa /
si khron mi rigs dpe skrun khang /
gleng gzhi /
bod rigs ni rang rgyal gyi lo rgyus yun ring ldan pa'i mi rigs rlabs chen zhig yin la /
las la brtson zhing dpa' ba dang /
blo rig ldan pa zhig kyang red /
rlabs chen gyi mes rgyal gsar gtod byed pa'i go rim nang du byas rjes 'od stong 'bar ba bzhag yod cing /
lo rgyus 'phel rgyas kyi chu klung ring po 'di'i nang du bod kyi mi rigs dang mi rigs gzhan dag thun mong thog nas mes rgyal gyi rig gzhung 'od stong rab tu 'phro ba zhig gsar gtod byas yod pa red /
bod yig gi dpe rnying 'di dag ni mes rgyal mi rigs kyi rig gzhung gi nor mdzod nang gi mu tig gzi 'od rab tu 'phro ba zhig red /
bod yig gi dpe rnying de dag dus rabs bcu gcig pa'i gong la sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab bsgyur rgyu de gtso bor byas shing /
de ni bod kyi btsan po mes dbon rnam gsum gyi dus nas 'go tshugs pa zhig red /
btsan po khri srong lde btsan gyi skabs su bsgyur zin pa'i gsung rab thams cad dkar chag tu bkod pa 'phang thang ma dang /
mchims phu ma /
ldan dkar ma gsum yod rung 'phang mchims gnyis kyi dkar chag 'thor gyar du song bas ldan dkar ma tsam las ma sus pa de ni bstan 'gyur gyi sna tshogs zhes pa'i khrod du bzhugs pa 'di yin /
dkar chag 'di'i nang bka' bstan gnyis sde tshan bcu dgur phyes te theg chen dang /
theg dman /
mdo phyogs /
sngags phyogs /
sde snod gsum bcas kyi go rim ltar phye thog mdo sde'i sde snod nang phar phyin dang /
phal chen /
dkon brtsegs /
bsdus pa chen po bcas kyi go rim ltar bsgrigs 'dug de ni gsung rab sde tshan dbye ba'i srol thog mar gtod pa zhig red /
bod la sangs rgyas chos lugs dar ba dang chabs cig chos lugs grub mtha' 'dra min 'ga' re byung ba'i 'go tshugs shing /
dus rabs bcu gcig pa tshun tsam la gsung rab de dag gi dgongs 'grel dang /
lo rgyus /
skad yig rig gnas skor sogs kyi rtsom  rigs je mang du phyin te rtsom rigs kyi glegs bam ha cang mang po zhig dar pa red /
da dag ni bod yig gi dpe rnying nang gi grub cha gal chen zhig red /
nang don mdor bsdus na rig gnas che ba lnga ste bzo rig pa dang /
gso ba rig pa /
sgra rig pa /
gtan tshigs rig pa /
nang don rig pa bcas dang /
rig gnas chung ba lnga ste snyan ngag dang /
mngon brjod /
sdeb sbyor /
zlos gar /
skar rtsis bcas yod pa red /
lhag par du lo rgyus dang rnam thar skor gyi rtsom rigs mang tsam zhig yod pa de'i nang nas bstan rtsis re'u mig dang /
rgyal rabs /
mi rigs bar gyi 'brel ba'i skor gyi lo rgyus /
chos 'byung /
grub mtha' so so'i bla rgyud /
gdung rabs /
rang rnam /
gsang ba'i rnam thar sogs dang /
gnas yig dang /
dgon pa'i gdan rabs sogs yod par ma zad /
gzhan yang mgur ma dang /
legs bshad /
tshig spel ma'i snyan ngag gi gtam rgyud sogs kyang yod la /
gna' dus rgya gar gyi skad yig saM skr-i ta'i sgra rig pa dang /
gtan tshigs rig pa /
snyan ngag sogs gsal bshad byed pa'i mchan 'grel skor gyi rtsom rigs kyang mi nyung ba zhig yod pa red /
de dag khyon yongs kyi grangs 'bor ji tsam yod pa ni re re bzhin brjod kyis mi lang ngo /
gong gsal rig gnas shul bzhag 'di dag ni bod kyi sangs rgyas chos lugs dang bod rigs kyi rig gzhung la brtag dpyad byed rgyur blangs na rdzogs rgyu med pa dang spyad na 'dzad mtha' med pa'i bang mdzod cig yin pas rang cag gis brtsi mthong chen po byed 'os pa zhig red /
gsung 'bum skor gyi rtsom rigs ni bka' bstan 'gyur gyi khongs su ma gtogs pa'i dpe rnying rtsom rigs kyi grub cha gtso bo zhig yin la bod yig dpe rnying gi bcud lta bu red /
dus rabs bco brgyad pa'i mjug la klong rdol bla ma ngag dbang blo bzang gis <bka' gdams pa dang dge lugs pa'i bla ma rags rim gyi gsung 'bum mtshan tho> bsgrigs pa de'i nang la gsung 'bum khag bzhi bcu tsam las /
bu ston rin chen grub dang /
rje tsong kha pa sogs mkhas dbang kha shas kyi gsung 'bum le tshan dpe tho zhib phra tsam dang /
de min mdor bsdus shig bkod 'dug cing /
dus rabs bcu dgu pa'i dkyil la drung chen shes rab rgya mtshos <dpe rgyun dkon pa 'ga' zhig gi tho yig don gnyer yid kyi kun dA bzhad pa'i  zla 'od 'bum gyi snye ma> zhes pa bsgrigs pa de'i nang du sde tshan bcu gnyis su phyes te gsung 'bum khag dgu bcu'i mtshan tho bkod 'dug lor bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du snum par thog dkod pa'i <bla brang dgon pa'i dpe cha spyi'i dkar chag> nang la sde khag che ba bcu bdun bgos shing /
gsung 'bum skor la mkhas dbang yi dpe tho bkod 'dug bod rigs kyi rig gnas bya gzhag shul 'dzin dang dar spel byed rgyu dang /
mi rigs khag gi rig gnas brje res byed rgyu /
thun mong du dar rgyas phun sum tshogs pa yong bar skul spel gtong rgyu /
mi rigs kyi tshan rigs zhib 'jug gi bya ba byed rgyu /
dngos po dang bsam blo'i dpal yon gnyis kyi 'dzugs skrun byed rgyu bcas la zhabs 'degs zhu ba'i ched du 'di ga dpe mdzod khang gi bod yig dpe rnying legs sgri byed pi rmang bzhi'i thog 'di gar bzhugs yod pa'i bod yig dpe rnying nang gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag zhib phra bsgrigs nas /
thog mar deb 'di bsgrigs pa yin /
deb 'di'i nang khyon bsdoms mkhas dbang brgya dang brgyad cu rtsam gyi gsung 'bum 'dus yod cing /
deb gsum du bgos te rim pas par bskrun byed rgyu yin /
gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag 'di ni dpe cha dang dpyad gzhi sogs 'tshol bde ched bod rgya skad gnyis shan sbyar byas nas bkod yod pa'i lag cha lta bu'i deb cig yin /
'on kyang 'di ga'i dpe mdzod khang du yod pa'i dpe cha'i gnas tshul mtshon pa tsam zhig las /
bod yig dpe rnying nang gsung 'bum skor gyi rtsom rigs yod do cog gi rnam pa yongs su mtshon mi thub /
bod yig dpe rnying rnams la dpe ming rgyas pa dang bsdus pa gnyis yod cing /
dpe ming rgyas pa de dag ha cang ring bas blor nges dka' ba dang /
lhag par du thun mong ma yin pa'i khyad chos dmigs bsal re yod la /
tha snyad dang mngon brjod rnam grangs mang bas klog pa pos go dka' ba zhig dang /
dpe ming kha byang bsdus pa de dag ni ming 'dra ba mang bas dkar chag bzo dus rnyog 'dzing yong sla ba zhig red /
der brten dpe cha'i kha byang yongs rdzogs ji bzhin bshus nas dkar chag bzos yod /
nga tshos ched dmigs kyis rtsom pa po so so'i gnas tshul mdor bsdus re ngo sprod zhus yod /
de'i nang rtsom pa po 'ga' zhig gi rnam thar sogs dpyad gzhi 'dzom po zhig ma rnyed  stabs gsan yig dang /
mjug byang /
bla brgyud sogs 'brel yod dpyad gzhir brten nas ngo sprad byas yod /
rtsom pa po 'ga' zhig la dpyad gzhi ma rnyed stabs bar stong la 'jog dgos byung /
dkar chag 'di bzo ba'i go rim nang la pe cin dpe mdzod khang dang /
krung dbyang mi rigs skad yig yig sgyur cus /
mi rigs dpe skrun khang /
krung dbyang mi rigs slob grwa chen mo /
mtsho sngon mi rigs slob grwa chen mo /
bod ljongs mi rigs slob grwa chen mo /
si khron mi rigs dpe skrun khang sogs 'brel yod las khungs khag nas rgyab skyor shugs chen gnang bar snying thag pa nas thugs rje che zhu rgyu yin /
nga tshos bod r+ya shan sbyar gyi dkar chag che gras 'di 'dra zhig bsgrigs pa thengs dang po yin pas nyams myong mi 'dang ba dang /
mi shugs mi 'dang ba /
bod kyi rig gnas khyab khongs kyi yon tshad dma' ba bcas la brten skyon dang nor 'khrul yod nges la mkhas dbang rnam pa dang /
klog pa po rnams kyis mdzub ston gnang ba'i re 'dun zhu rgyu bcas /
...  ...  dkar chag sgrig tshul skor gyi gsal bshad /
dkar chag 'di ni gsung 'bum gyi rtsom pa po so so'i mtshan zur las dras pa'i ka kha'i go rim ltar bsgrigs yod /
grub mtha'i bla brgyud dang sku rabs grags che ba rnams de'i go rim ji bzhin mtshon par byed ched /
spyi ming bkod yod pa dper na karma pa sku phreng rim byon gyi gsung 'bum la !!ka yig'' dang /
tA la'i sku phreng rim byon gyi gsung 'bum la !!tA yig'' sa skya'i gong ma lnga'i gsung 'bum la !!sa yig'' bcas gzhir bzhag nas ka mad rim pa ltar bsgrigs shing /
bla brgyud dang sku rabs so so'i nang khul gyi rtsom pa po'i mtshan ni sku phreng snga phyi'i go rim ltar bsgrigs yod /
gsung 'bum tshar rer par ma'am bris ma gang rung zhig la cha bzhag nas /
sngon gyi glegs bam dang dpe tshan bsgrigs tshul sor bzhag thog par gzhi gzhan la'ang zur bltas byas te /
ma tshang ba rnams kha skong byas yod /
dper na dngul chu dbyangs can grub pa'i rdo rje'i gsung 'bum ga pod nang ang grangs rtags can rnams ni par gzhi gzhan nas drangs pa'i rtags yin /
'ga' zhig ni logs su bsgrigs yod /
par gzhi mi 'dra ba'i nang la nang don 'dra yang kha byang mi 'dra ba yod pa dper na tsong kha pa'i gsung 'bum kha pod nang la lha sa'i par mar lam rim la <skyes bu gsum gyi nyams su blangs pa'i byang chub lam gyi rim pa bzhugs so> zhes 'khod pa dang /
sde dge'i par mar <rgyal ba'i gsung rab thams cad kyi snying po'i gnad bsdus te gtan la phab pa byang chub lam gyi rim pa bzhugs so> zer ba lta bu kha byang mi 'dra ba rnams so sor bkod yod /
nang don mi 'dra yang kha byang mtshungs pa dper na <kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po rig 'dzin 'jigs med gling pa'i bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs kyi bzhugs byang chos rab rnam 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs /
> rtags can nang gi par gsal ba de  rigs kyang so sor bkod yod /
nang don 'dra la kha byang yang de tsam dbye ba cher med pas dbye 'byed sla tsam yod pa rnams gcig gis 'thus pa byas yod /
po ti so so'i gdong tshal la yod pa'i ang grangs dang kha bskong du drangs pa'i dpe tshan so so'i gsham la yod pa'i ang grangs ni rang re'i dpe mdzod khang gi pod grangs mtshon byed yin /
dpe tshan gsham gyi rtags yod pa 'di ni po ti de'i nang gi dpe tshan gyi go rim mtshon pa'i ang grangs yin /
rtags kyi rgyab la yod pa'i ang ki de ni shog grangs mtshon byed yin /

karma pa sku phreng gsum pa rang byung rdo rje ni /
gtsang stod skyid grong 'phags pa wa ti'i lha khang gi lho phyogs gangs zhur mo zhes par yab chos dpal dang /
yum jo mo g.yang 'dren gnyis kyi sras su rab byung lnga pa'i shing pho sprel lor 'khrungs /
dgung lo lnga par grub chen o rgyan pa rin chen dpal mjal bar byon /
grub chen pas /
nga'i bla ma'i gsang mtshan rang byung rdo rje yin pas de ka 'dogs gsungs nas rang byung rdo rjer mtshan gsol /
dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang sems bskyed gnang /
dgung lo bdun par khro phu shes rab kyis mkhas po mdzad de dge tshul bsgrubs /
'dul ba gsan /
rta lor sa g.yos byung ba'i shing rta lo'i rjes kyi lo shas de'i nang la gnas brtan gzhon nu 'byung bas mkhan po dang /
dge 'dun rin chen gyis las slob mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs /
'dul ba yongs rdzogs gsan /
slob dpon shes rab dpal /
rgya sgom ye shes /
snye mdo kun dga' don grub sogs las bod kyi yul du bka' bstan 'gyur ro 'tshal thams cad gsan par mdzad /
de nas karma'i gdan sar byon /
sa skya 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan der phebs pa dang mjal nas gsung gleng mdzad /
kha ba dkar por byon nas gnas yig brtsams /
de nas kam po gnas nang du byon /
chu glang lor tsA rir phebs /
zla ba gsum bzhugs /
mtshur phur tshur phebs /
shing bya lor kong por gdan drangs /
der sgrub sde 'ga' zhig btab /
mdo khams su byon /
sog chur lcags zam btsugs /
de nas hor rgyal pos gdan 'dren byas /
lcags lug lor gser yig pa mgon po tshim ching sogs dbus su slebs pas chos rje kong po nas gdan drangs /
gdan zhu'i 'ja' sa bsgrags /
sa skya'i ti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan nas mes rgyal nang khul du phebs dgos tshul zhus /
kun rgyan pa rang nyid sngon du phebs /
chu sprel lo'i zla gnyis pa'i tshes gcig la stod lung mtshur phu nas bteg zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la rgyal po gshegs nas mjal ma thub kyang /
chu sprel zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bco brgyad la pho brang chen por 'byor /
rgyal bu rat na shri sogs kyis bsu ba rgya chen po byas /
de rjes rgyal bu yang 'das /
de'i gcen po tho gan the mur sman rtse'i yul nas gdan drangs /
de nas rgyal po tho gan the mur dang btsun mo blon po sogs la dbang bskur chos bshad gnang /
de nas shing khyi'i lor chos rje bod du phebs khar tshal pa si tu dge sbyong chen po la go shri'i ming dang shel tham /
mtshur phu dang karma pa sogs la bdag rkyen dang bod spyi la phan pa'i 'ja' sa gsum /
bstan 'gyur bzhengs pa'i cha rkyen sogs phul nas bod du yar byon /
shing phag lo'i zla ba brgyad par 'dam du phebs /
bod kyi che dgus bsus /
'ja' sa gsum po bsgrags /
bod du phebs nas gser dngul gyis bstan 'gyur po ti brgya dang drug cu bzhengs /
me byi lor gdan 'dren gser yig pa gsum pa slebs /
zla ba brgyad par slar yang rgya nag tu byon nas /
me glang lo'i zla gsum pa'i tshes gcig la pho brang chen por phebs /
phebs bsu mthong bkur sogs sngar bas kyang che /
gser bre bzhi sogs 'bul ba phul /
sa g.yos chen po byung skabs chos rje dang gong ma mchod yon gnyis thang du gzims gur phub nas bzhugs pas nyes skyon ma byung /
dgung grangs nga drug tu phebs pa sa yos lo'i zla drug pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la zhi bar gshegs /
chos rje 'di la slob ma grags che ba zhwa dmar grags pa seng ge mkhas grub g.yung ston pa /
rta sna go shri kun rgyal /
tshal pa si tu /
g.yag sde pan chen /
kun mkhyen dol po pa sogs mang ngo /
gsung rab ni ston pa'i skyes rabs dang /
zab mo nang don gyi rtsa 'grel sogs po ti ka kha gnyis dang /
bris ma pod gcig bcas nged dpe mdzod khang du pod gsum bzhugs so /

karma mi bskyod rdo rje'i gsung 'bum / /
... bris ma /
... ga phrin yig bstod tshogs dris lan bslab bya smon lam rnams kyi dkar chag /
... lha sa'i jo bo la phul ba'i zhu yig /
... gangs ri'i khrod na gnas pa gtso bor gyur pa skyabs med ma rgan gyi tshogs la sha zar mi rung ba'i springs yig sogs bzhugs so / /
... rtogs ldan rin po che zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa lnga pa sprul sku thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog 'bangs kyi rnam par thar pa bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzad pa bcu gnyis la bstod pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bstod pa bzhugs so / /
... dris lan rnams bzhugs so / /
... gsang sngags snga 'gyur las 'phros pa'i brgal lan rtsod pa med pa'i ston pa dang bstan pa'i byung ba brjod pa drang po'i sa bon zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  karma phrin las gnyis pa la chos sbyin du bstsal ba'o / /
... rje mnyam pa grub chen gyi gsung thor bu 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
... gdul bya phyi ma la gdams pa bzhugs so / /
... dad ldan 'ga' zhig la bslab byar gdams pa bzhugs so / /
... bshad gsar ba kun la mchod yar du gdams pa bzhugs so / /
... karma kam tshang gi bsam gtan pa'i dge 'dun sder longs su bzhugs pa rnams la khrims su bcas pa'o / /
... karma bka' brgyud kyi spong ba bsam gtan pa rnams la gtso bor gyur pa'i dben pa dang tshogs su bzhugs pa dang khyad par dge 'dun sder longs rnams la kun spyod rags pa khrigs su bcas pa bzhugs so / /

karma pa sku phreng brgyad pa mi bskyod rdo rje ni /
chab mdo'i nub byang ngos kyi ngom chu rgyud g.yas lung kar ti phug pa tam zer bar yab a byams dang /
yum bla ma sgron gnyis kyi sras su rab byung dgu pa'i me yos lor sku 'khrungs /
zla ngo bdun bzhes pa na ri bo cher byon /
bsnyen bkur cher zhus /
de nas lho rong rdzong du spyan drangs pa ltar byon /
dgung lo lnga tsam la phebs dus /
rgyal tshab bkra shis rnam rgyal dang ri bo che'i mi sna lho rong gi go shri sogs nas karma pa'i sku phreng yin par thag bcad /
de nas chu bya lor khri 'don byas /
rgyal tshab rin po che bkra shis rnam rgyal 'di mtshur phu rgyal tshab sprul sku zer ba'i sku thog dang po de yin /
las theg chen so thar gyi sdom pa bzhes te mtshan chos kyi grags pa dpal bzang por gsol /
yi ge 'bri klog la brtson par mdzad /
de nas mdo khams shar phyogs su byon /
dgung lo brgyad pa la zur mang mtsho sngon lho rgyud skye rgu mdo'i lho nub dang nye bar zur mang che chung gnyis yod pa de'o /
du byon /
de nas 'dan ma grub chen sangs rgyas mnyan ras nas byang chub gling du gdan drangs /
zhwa khra can stong phrag lhag gis bsu ba byas /
de nas kam po gangs rar kam po gnas nang phebs shing /
'jang sa tham rgyal pos gdan 'dren byung bas rim par byon /
me byi lor sa tham du phebs /
bsu ba la rgyal po nyid gyam khrir phebs /
khu bo dang nu bo gnyis glang chen zhon /
glang chen gcig yan par khrid /
rta pa mang pos gdugs dang rgyal mtshan thogs nas bsu ba bya /
pho brang du spyan drangs te bkur bzos bla lhag tu byas /
sa tham rgyal pos bod la lo bcu gsum bar dmag khral dang bu khral btsun khral lo ltar lnga brgya re phul /
dgon pa brgya 'debs par khas blangs /
[me byi 'di nas brtsis pa'i lo re bzhi tsam song pa'i lor tA la'i gsum pa bsod nams rgya mtshos li thang du li thang theg chen chos 'khor gling btab /
de dus sbyin bdag sa tham rgyal pos byas pa'i lo rgyus bai ser dang li thang dgon par tA la'i bdun pas bstsal pa'i bka' shog dang bca' yig nang 'khod pa ngo ma zhig dngos su mthong bas zur 'debs kyi tshul du bris so /
] sa tham du zhag bdun bzhugs /
lo bdun mtshams nas 'byon par zhal bzhes gnang /
skyel ma dang bcas tshur byon /
sa tham rgyal pos rgyal tshab gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs su dge 'dun par gser zho re 'gyed dang /
gdung rten bzhengs rgyur gser zho lnga brgya /
zangs dos bcu /
thub chen gser thog rgyur zangs dos sum cu /
gser zho ltong r+wa can /
ja brgya sogs gnang /
de nas dkar mdzes khul gyi nyag chu gru kha sogs brgyud nas phebs /
'dan ma grub chen sangs rgyas mnyan ras kyi mdun nas dgung lo bcu par dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /
chos bka' dbang lung ci rigs gsan /
de nas 'dan khog byang chub gling du byon /
sangs rgyas mnyan pas sgar pa stong phrag gi phog phul /
der lo gsum tsam bzhugs nas dbang lung khrid gsum gsan /
sa yos tsam la rgya nag tu phebs dgos pa'i gser yig pa 'byor yang ma phebs /
de nas kong por byon /
kong po bu chur rgyal tshab sprul sku'i gtsug phud bzhes /
mtshan grags pa dpal 'byor zhes pa gnang /
mon rgyal pos gser ljang rdung gi pad zhu phul /
dgung lo nyer gcig par mkhan chen chos grub seng ge dang slob dpon karma 'phrin las pa sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs /
mkhan slob gnyis kyi mdun nas bka' chos mang du gsan /
karma lo tsA ba rin chen bkra shis las sgra dang sum rtags sogs gsan /
de dus skabs shig la phrag yul sogs yon mchod thams cad gros mthun gyis kong po khul gyi dge lugs dgon sde brlag par brtsam pa na /
chos rjes bkag par mdzad /
de ltar khams kong khul rgyun ring tsam bzhugs nas dgung lo so gcig par mtshur phur byon /
de dus dbus gtsang gi bar chings mdzad /
sku tshe'i mjug tu tsA rir gnas skor phebs nas dgung lo zhe brgyad bzhes pa'i shing stag lo'i zla ba brgyad par lho kha yar klung du zhi ngar gshegs so /

mtsho sngon lho rgyud rtse gzhung gi sa cha'i bye brag dang po'i mdo  zhes pa'i yul du rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa mo bya'i lo la 'khrungs /
sku bltams nas yun mi ring bar yab bde chen nas 'phrin las rdo rje zhes pa'i mtshan gsol /
dgung grangs lnga par phebs skabs /
'jam bzhad sku phreng gsum pa 'jigs med rgya mtsho mchog nas /
rong po chos rje'i sku skye ru ngos 'dzin mdzad /
blo bzang 'phrin las bstan pa rgya mtsho zhes pa'i mtshan bstsal /
dgung lo drug pa nas a lags bstan pa yongs 'dzin du bsten /
'bri klog sogs slob 'go tshugs /
bla brang bkra shis 'khyil gyi 'du khang chen mor khri ston mdzad /
dge bshes thub bstan mtha' yas la mdo sngags kyi gzhung mang po gsan pa dang /
rje dkon mchog smon lam bzang po'i mdun nas rab tu byung /
dgung lo brgyad par dkon mchog smon lam mdun dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /
dgung lo bcu gcig pa nas nyer bzhi'i bar yongs 'dzin dang mtshan zhabs pa dge bshes chen po rnams kyi mdun nas gzhung pod lnga la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad /
dgung lo nyer bzhi par rang gi gdan sar rje btsun ngag dbang chos 'phel mdun bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes /
rab byung bco lnga pa'i chu mo bya'i lor si khron rnga pa'i yul du dgon gsar phal cher btab grub cing dgon de'i gdan sar bzhugs te /
bshad grwa dang sgrub grwa btsugs te bstan pa rgya cher spel /
dgung lo nga drug tu phebs pa rab byung bco lnga pa'i shing mo sbrul gyi lo la rang dgon du sku gsheggs so /

mdo smad kyi dgon sde phal mo che dang /

lha rams dge bshes shes rab rgya mtsho ni /
mtsho sngon rdo sbis gser mug ljongs kyi sa'i char gtogs pa hor grong pa zhes pa'i grong sde der yab lha lung skyabs dang /
yum lha lung skyid gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bco lnga pa'i shing pho sprel gyi lo'i zla ba bzhi pa'i yar ngor sku bltams /
dgung lo lnga pa'i tshe 'bras spungs sgo mang dge bshes lha rams pa nor bu rin po che'i drung nas rab byung dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /
dge ldan 'phel rgyas gling gi chos sgor zhugs nas yi ge sbyor klog la sbyang pa legs par mdzad /
dgung lo bcu drug pa'i ston khar chos sde chen po bla brang bkra shis 'khyil gyi chos grwar zhugs te slob gnyer la brtson pa chen po mdzad /
a khu gung thang blo gros dang /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa sku phreng bzhi pa bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug sogs mkhas pa mang po bsten /
a khu gung thang blo gros tshang gi mdun nas dge slong gi sdom pa mnos /
dgung lo nyer gcig par khong dbus su phebs te 'bras spungs sgo mang grwa tshang gi chos sgor zhugs shing /
mdo sngags rig gnas yongs su rdzogs pa'i mkhas pa'i dbang po mchog grub dkar po dang /
bla ma 'bul sdud rin po che blo bzang ye shes bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen bcu phrag gsum lhag spyi bo'i cod pan du bsten te rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag la thos bsam mthar phyin par mdzad nas 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi mdzad pa rgya cher spel /
dgung lo so gsum gyi steng dmigs bsal gyis lha rams 'phar ma'i ming btags blangs /
nor bu gling ga'i rtsod rgyugs skabs ang dang po thob /
rtse'i gzim chung du tshogs langs dmigs bsal can gnang ba sogs mkhas grags kyi rtsal thon /
lo der smon lam gyi grwa skor ba rnams dam bca' ang rim sgrig skabs /
tA la'i bcu gsum pa'i bka' don ltar rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas pa ang dang po 'bras spungs sgo mang klu 'bum dge bshes shes rab rgya mtsho zhes mtshan snyan gyi me tog dgung du 'thor /
dgung lo sum cu so bzhi par tA la'i bcu gsum pa'i bka' ltar bu ston rin chen grub kyi gsung 'bum pod nyer drug skor yod pa par gzhi gsar bzhengs kyi zhu dag dang /
de rjes bka' 'gyur lha sa par gsar gyi zhu dag mdzad /
khong la slob ma yang ha cang mang po yod /
grags che ba dge bshes lha rams pa skal bzang rgyam tsho dang /
dge bshes gzhung pa  tshul khrims rgya mtsho sogs dang /
de min slob gnyer la don gnyer byed mkhan mang po la sgra /
snyan ngag sum rtags sogs khrid nas bskyed bsrings mdzad de bod kyi rig gnas mi nyams gong spel gyi bya ba mang po zhig mdzad /
dgung lo nga lngar phebs tshe mes rgyal nang khul du phebs /
de nas krung hwa mi dmangs spyi mthun rgyal khab dbu brnyes rjes bod zhi bas bcing 'grol ched du 'bad pa lhod med mdzad /
nang pa'i chos tshogs kyi tshogs gtso'i go gnas bzhes /
dgung lo don gsum par rgya gar dang /
bal po rgyal khab gnyis kyis gdan zhus ltar shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo nyis stong lnga brgya'i rjes dran tshogs chen la zhugs /

can pu'u kre /

... many+dzu badzra gyi zin bris bzhugs so / /
...  sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba'i dka' ba'i gnas rnam par 'byed pa zhib mo rnam 'thag ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstan bcos sdom gsum gyi gnas gsum gsal bar byed pa nor bu chu shel bzhugs so / /
... yul chen po bdun gyi ngos 'dzin 'khrul med gsal ba ces bya ba bzhugs / /
... tsA ri dang de wi ko Ta'i yul gyi dgag sgrub bzhugs / /
...  sdom gsum rab dbye'i bde gshegs snying po'i gsal byed / /
...  sdom gsum bsgrag zung gi thad kyi gsung rgyun bzhugs so / /
...  sems bskyed kyi cho ga bzhugs so / /
... na ro pa nas brgyud pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed kyi phyag len rnams bzhugs so / /
... bla ma dpal skyabs la gnang ba'i blo sbyong theg mchog gnad kyi snying po bzhugs so / /
... thub pa dgongs gsal gyi 'chad thabs bzhugs so / /
... thub pa dgongs pa gsal ba zhes bya ba'i gzhung gi bshad thabs rgyal sras lam bzang gi mdzes rgyan bzhugs so / /
... rgyal sras lam bzang gi sgrung 'grel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...   bris ma /
... ga bsod nams lhun grub bka' 'bum ga pa'i dkar chag bzhugs / /
...  'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gsung gi lan rnam par gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dbu ma chos kyi dbyings su bstod pa'i rnam par bshad pa don dam snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... snying po'i don gsal bar byed pa lung gi phreng ba bzhugs so / /
... pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam gyi rnam par bzhag pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bslab btus kyi legs 'grel bzhugs so / /
... bsgom rim bar pa'i sa bcad bzhugs so / /
... yum gyi 'dres rkang bzhugs so / /
... mdo kun las btus pa'i sa bcad bzhugs so / /
... yas gtam 'bras bu rin po che rnam par spel ba dngos grub kyi gter bzhugs so / /
... chos rje rnam rgyal ba'i dris lan bzhugs so / /
... chos rje rnam rgyal ba la gnang ba'i dris lan rtsa rgyud kyi dka' ba'i gnas cung zad bzhugs so / /
...  chos rje rnam rgyal dpal bzang po'i dris lan bzhugs so / /
...  gnas gsum gsal byed las 'phros pa'i dris lan bzhugs so / /
...  dris lan don gsum gsal byed bzhugs so / /
... byang pa mchod gnas pa'i dris lan nges don snying po bzhugs so / /
... mtsho byed chos skyong dpal bzang gi dris lan bzhugs so / /
...  mi'i dbang po mgon po rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan rgyal sras bzhad pa'i me tog bzhugs so / /
... mi'i dbang po mgon po rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan padma'i snying po bzhugs so / /
... mi'i dbang po mgon po rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan sngon rabs gsal ba'i me long bzhugs so / /
... dpon btsun kun dga' dpal bzang grogs mched kyi zhus lan bzhugs so / /
... zha lu lo tsA ba la dri ba mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal gyis dris pa'i lan bzhugs so / /
... rtsa ba'i bla ma'i dris lan bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun sa skya paN+Ti chen po la 'phrin du gsol ba bzhugs so / /
...  rje nyid kyi thugs la 'khrungs pa'i tshigs bcad bzhugs so / /
...  skal ldan snying gi mun sel lha dbang rdo rje zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun mi la ras pas mthar thug gi lta ba ji ltar bzhed lugs 'khrul med snang ba / /
... rang la bskul ba tshig zur brgyad pa zhes bya ba dge / /
... chos rgyal nor bu la phul ba'i zhu yig bzhugs so / /
... mi dbang bkra shis mgon la phul ba dge / /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba dge / /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba'i zhu yig /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba skabs gnyis snang /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la gdams pa bzhugs so / /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba bzhugs so / /
... a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba dge / /
... dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la gdams pa / /
...  drung blo pa la gdams pa bzhugs / /
... yid las byung ba'i tshigs bcad bzhugs so / /
... rdo rje 'dzin dbyangs kyi 'grel pa zhi 'tshos mdzad pa las btus pa dge / /
... mi'i dbang po a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba bzhugs / /
...  mgo sngon gyi mjug gi shis brjod bzhugs so / /
... rin po che chen mo'i dgongs rdzogs kyi mchod brjod bstan rtsis dang bcas pa / /
... chos rgyal chen po bkra shis mgon gyi sa skya'i dgongs rdzogs kyi mchod brjod bzhugs / /
... bdag chen ma gur r+g+y+la gyi brgyad stong pa'i dkar chag /
...  mdo mang gser gyi glegs bam 'bum phrag gi /
mtshon byed rin chen ngag gi lde mig can /
shis brjod sgo gsum ldan pa'i snyan tshig gis /
mkhas mang yid kyi shing rta dga' bzhugs so / /
... rin po che bde rgyal ba'i brgyad stong pa'i dkar chag /
...  u dum brtag gnyis kyi dkar chag /
... bdag mo sangs rgyas sgron gyi gdung chos brgyad stong pa'i mtshon byed bzhugs / /
...  bsam grub gling gi gser khang gi dkar chag bzhugs so / /
...  dkar chag rin po che'i sgron ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... chos zom 'du khang gi lha tshogs kyi dkar chag dag / /

... phun tshogs bsam gtan gling gi gser khang lha khang gi dkar chag bkra shis so / /
... skye rtsa bla mas sa skya bka' 'bum sogs bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed / /
... sa skya bka' 'bum /

... bde legs gling gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed bzhugs / /
... brgyad tog gser gsum gyi dkar chag bzhugs / /

... bris ma /
... bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag rin po che'i phreng ba bzhugs so / /

sa skya bla ma bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas ni /
rab byung bdun pa'i lcags mo bya'i lo la 'khrungs shing /
khong ni sa kya drung chen pa la sras spun mched bzhi yod pa'i nang /
spun tha chung yin /
sku mched gsum pos srid skyong ba'i bya ba mdzad cing /
khong chos lam du zhugs te /
dgung lo gnyis par yum dang lhan cig 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho'i mdun nas skyabs 'gro'i sdom pa dang /
gtsug gtor rnam par rgyal ba'i rjes gnang sogs zhag bdun gyi ring la zhus /
dgung lo gsum pa'i dus su bsod nams rgyal mtshan drung du tshe dbang zhus /
dgung lo lnga drug gi dus su rnying ma ba dge legs rgyal mtshan drung du /
tshe dbang dang /
gu ru bka' brgyad kyi dbang sogs dbang mang du zhus /
dgung lo dgu par yon tan chos rgyal gyi  drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug mdun nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos /
rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug gis /
chos rje ra chen pa slob dpon du bskos /
de'i mdun nas phar phyin dang tshad ma lo drug sbyangs /
de nas lo gnyis tsam ring /
chos rje yon tan chos rgyal dang tshul khrims rgyal mtshan sogs kyi drung du /
dbu ma dang /
sdom gsum rab dbye /
rdo rje'i gur dang /
gsang 'dus sogs mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs kun la gsan sbyong mthar phyin mdzad /
thub chen rnam rgyal gtsug lag khang du /
mkhan chen yon tan chos rgyal gtsos dge 'dun 'dus pa dgu brgya lhag gi mdun sar nyin gsum ring phar phyin /
rnam 'grel /
sdom gsum /
dbu ma bcas po ti bzhi'i bshad pa sa lugs kyi sgros ltar mdzad pas /
dge 'dun yongs kyis legs so byin /
dgung lo nyi shu par rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug drung du dge slong gi sdom pa zhus /
de nas yun mi ring par bla ma kun dga' dbang phyug sku gshegs /
de rjes gdan sa 'dzin mkhan sde pa 'jam dbyangs dang khong gi bar sel bcug nas 'gal ba byung zhing grub mtha' yang cung zad mi 'dra bar gyur /
lan gnyis tsam gnas gzhan du 'gro bar brtsams kyang slob ma rnams nas ma mngags /
khong der bzhugs ring chos rje grags pa rgyal mtshan drung du dam chos kyi dga' ston tshad med myangs /
lo 'ga'i ring skyabs 'gro sogs la 'bad cing /
lkog tu 'chad nyan cung zad re'ang mdzad de bzhugs /
skabs de dag tu sde pa 'jam dbyangs nas grwa rigs rnams la chad las sogs mi rigs pa sna tshogs byed par yid skyo zhing /
mthar 'chad nyan dang grub mtha'i bshad pa sogs dor yang /
ma phan par 'jig rten tha mal ba ltar rtsod gleng byed dgos byung bas /
bya thabs bral te /
gtsang gi gnas gzhan du phebs dgos par thug e waM du phebs nas lo 'gar bzhugs /
de nas sa skyar sde pa 'jam dbyangs 'das zin rjes /
mi'i dbang po nam mkha' bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyis /
khong la de gar phebs dgos kyi bka' lung gnang ba dang /
sde pa chung ba khong dang bzang bar yod pa des kyang yong dgos gsungs par brten /
khong sa skyar phebs nas /
'chad nyan nyams len gyi bya ba mdzad /
'on kyang skabs der /
sa ngor bar dang /
gser mdog can dang /
sde pa gzhis ka ba'i bar 'khrug rtsod tshabs chen byung las /
'jigs pa chen pos mnar /
de nas yun mi ring bar sa g.yos te /
rtsi shing nags tshal thams cad nyams shing /
dge 'dun gyi sde dang gtsug lag khang phal mo che'ang zhig rten khyad 'phags rnams kyang ma rungs par gyur /
sems can grangs med pa zhig kyang tshe'i dus byas nas yul thams cad 'brog dgon stong pa zhig tu re zhig gi bar lus so /
de nas yang gong gi bka' nan byung ba dang du blangs te lcags pho stag gi lo nas /
chu pho 'brug gi lo'i bar  lo gsum ring /
gdung brgyud rin po che la /
rang la thob tshad kyi dam chos phal mo che phul /
de nas rab byung dgu pa'i chu mo lug nas shing pho sprel bar zur bzhugs lo gnyis mdzad de rab byung dgu pa'i shing mo bya'i lo la 'das pa yin nam snyam /
khong gi gsung rab ni /
bstod pa'i tshogs dang /
rnam thar sna tshogs /
dris lan sogs bstan bcos mang po yod pa rnams gcig tu bsdus pa'i po ti sde dge'i par ma gnyis dang /
bris ma po ti bzhi bcas khyon nged dpe mdzod khang du po ti drug bzhugs yod lags /

klong chen rab 'byams pa dri med 'od zer gyi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /

...  yid bzhin mdzod kyi don khrid zab don rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... man ngag rin po che'i mdzod lo gsum ring /
gdng brgyad rin po che la /
rang la thob tshad kyi dam chos phal mo che phul /
de nas rab byung dgu pa'i chu mo lug na shing pho sprel bar zur bzhugs lo gnyis mdzad e rab byung dgi pa'i shing mo bya'i lo la 'das pa yin nam snyam /
khong gi gsung rab ni /
bstod pa'i tshogs dang /
rnam thar sna tshogs /
dris las sog s+b+s+tan bcos mang po yod pa rnams gcig tu bsdus pa'i po te sde dge'i par ma gnyis dang /
bris ma po te bzhi bcas khyon nged dpe mdzod khang du po ti drug bzhugs yod lags /

klong chen rab 'byams pa dri med 'od zer gyi gsung 'bu / /

... thig pa chen po'i man ngag gi bstan bcos yid bzhin rin po che'i mdzod kyi 'grel pa padma dkar po zhes bya ba bzhugs / /

yab tshong dpon pa sangs dang /
yum chung skyes gnyis las rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i lcags mo sbrul gyi lo la sku bltams /
dgung lo brgyad pa'i dus su bkra shis lhun por grwa btsun mdzad de /
paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma'i mdun rab tu byung zhing dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
sbyor klog legs par sbyangs /
dgung lo bcu gsum pa nas tshad ma sbyong ba'i dbu btsugs /
bsdus tshan gyi rgyugs phul bas dgyes bzhes dang chog bka' thob /
skabs der sgrig ha cang dam pa sogs kyi rkyen gyis sdod mos med stabs zhabs thang nas dbus su phebs /
yun ring ma 'gor bar rang shag tu tshur log gzhung pod lnga la 'bad pa mdzad /
bka' bcu'i ming rtags thob /
dgung lo nyer bdun par paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma'i mdun bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blangs /
dgung lo nyer dgu par rab 'byams smra ba'i seng ge'i mtshan rtags bzhes /
de nas rgyud pa grwa tshang du lo bcu gnyis kyi bar dbyangs rol sogs nas gsang sngags skor kun sbyangs /
'di'i skabs su yongs lho chen po dang dka' chen zhabs drung gnyis kyis lhan cig bgros nas khong yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin gyi sku skye yin 'dug ces bshad par brten /
dbus gtsang yong su gtam des khyab cing /
bka' zur mkhyen rab bsam gtan gyis yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin gyi bzhugs gnas dpal 'byor lhun po'i ri khrod du gdan zhu byas /
dgung lo zhe gcig par paN chen nas bkra shis lhun po'i dkyil khang grwa tshang gi gdan sar bskos /
dgung lo nga bdun par paN chen rin po che lha ldan du tA la'i bcu gsum pa thub bstan rgya mtshor dbu phud mtshan gsol sogs la phebs dus /
phyag phyir byon nas 'bras spungs dang se ra dgon sogs su mang 'gyed dang bla mchod khrid chos sogs phul /
mkhas pa rnams dang chos kyi bgros gleng mang po mdzad /
mkhas pa'i grags pa thob /
khong nam 'das pa rang rnam tshig bcad mar mi gsal bas /
dus gtan 'khel 'bri thabs bral /
'on kyang rang rnam 'di dgung lo don gcig tu phebs pa'i skabs su brtsams 'dug pas /
rang rnam brtsams rjes yun ring bzhugs med dam snyam mo /

khang gsar blo bzang tshul khrims bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan ni /

... dus gsum rgyal ba'i yum gcig dbyangs can lha mo la bstod pa dbyangs can dgyes pa skyed byed bstod sprin rgya mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs / /

... dpal mgon zhal gyi bstod pa lhun grub chos sku ma'i 'grel pa bzhugs so / /

... rgyun du kha 'don byed na nyams len 'ong ba'i man ngag zab mo bzhugs so / /
... bya dka' bzhi sdebs snyan ngag mdzes rgyan gyi bslab bya bzhugs so / /

yab klu 'bum yags dang yum lha mo mtsho gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gcig pa'i shing pho 'brug gi lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu dgu la 'khrungs /
dgung lo bdun par ka kha sogs 'bri klog sbyangs /
dge rgan don yod 'byung gnas mdun smon lam dang 'jam dpal mtshan brjod sogs sbyangs /
de dus lo lnga'i ring phyugs 'tsho zhor dang yig rtsa sbyong bzhin byas te dgung lo bcu gcig pa'i dus su /
bla ma ri khrod pa'i drung du rab tu byung zhing dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
ming blo gros rgya mtsho btags /
de nas ri khrod pa slob dpon du bsten nas dpe klog lo 'ga' song rjes /
co ne chos rje dbus su phebs pa dang lhan cig a khu shes rab don yod kyis skyel ma byas te dbus su  phebs /
'bras sgo mang grwa tshang du zhugs /
tshad ma'i rig pa la gsan sbyong mdzad /
bar mtshams su gtsang bkra shis lhun por gnas mjal phebs /
dbus su log rjes /
mkhan po pha bong kha pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin mdun bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje sogs bla ma mang po'i mdun chos mang du zhus /
de nas mi ring bar byang 'grul dang mnyam du a mdor tshur phebs /
dgon pa gsar 'debs rten gsar bzhengs sogs chos kyi bya ba rgya cher spel /
mdo smad dgon khag yongs su zhabs kyis bcags /
dgung lo mthon por phebs pa na ri khrod du 'tsho ba ngan ngon bsten nas nyams len kho na mdzad /
dgung lo bdun cu don bdun du phebs pa rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i lcags pho spre'u lo zla ba dang po'i tshes gsum nyin par dgongs pa chos dbyings su thims so / /

khong gis dar zhing gi gdan sa 'dzin /

dgung lo nyer lnga'i bar gzhung pod rnams la gsan sbyong mdzad /
mdo smad dgon khag tu phar phyin gyi grwa skor mdzad rjes /
rgyal mkhan po dang mnyam du dgung lo nyer drug par dbus su phebs /
'bras spungs sgo mang grwa tshang du sgo mang bla ma 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje'i mdun chos mang po zhus shing slob gnyer legs par mdzad /
dgung lo so drug par lha sa smon lam chen po'i thog dge 'dun khri phrag brgal ba'i dbus su gzhung pod lnga'i bshad pa dang rtsod pa byas pas /

rab 'byams pa'i ming rtags blangs /
dgung lo bzhi bcu par sde pa gzhung nas khong gtsang dpal 'khor chos sde'i mkhan por bskos /
de rjes rtse chen chos sde'i gdan sa'ang bzung nas /
dgon bzhengs gso dang sgrig lam kun spyod legs bcos /
chos 'chad nyan gyi srol gsar btsugs sogs chos kyi bya ba legs par mdzad cing /
paN chen blo bzang ye shes mdun dam pa'i chos mang du zhus /

de nas dgung lo lnga bcu nga lnga par mdo smad reb kong phyogs kyi rong po dgon du tshur phebs te gdan sa 'dzin /
mdo smad phyogs kyi dgon khag yongs su phebs shing 'chad nyan nyams len gyi bya ba rgya cher spel /
dgung lo brgyad cu gya bdun la phebs pa rab byung bcu gsum pa'i shing mo bya'i lo la 'das so /

mkhan po no mon han blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan ni /
rab byung bcu gcig pa'i sa mo yos kyi lo zla ba dang po'i tshes bco lnga la sog po'i dpon rigs kyi dud tshang zhig tu 'khrungs /
dgung lo lnga pa'i dus su /
nam mkha' bsod nams grags pa'i mdun dbang zhus /
ming chos kyi rdo rje btags /
dgung lo drug par /
bkra shis lhun po nas byon pa'i blo bzang yar 'phel mdun /
klog dang sbyor sdeb blo 'dzin rnams sbyangs /
dgung lo bdun par blo bzang yar 'phel mdun dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa zhus /
mtshan blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan gsol /
skabs der paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan nas /
khong grub chen rje dpon legs tshogs lhun grub kyi sku skye ru ngos 'dzin mdzad /
de nas chos rgyal 'phrin las rgya mtsho bla mar bsten nas /
dbang lung lag khrid sogs mang du zhus /
'phan yul sman pa kun dga' byang chub mdun du gso rig rtsa ba'i rgyud dang phyi ma'i rgyud /
skar rtsis /
sog yig sogs sbyangs /
de nas dbus gtsang du phebs /
dgon gnas yongs la mang 'gyed dang bla drags rnams la chos 'brel zhus /
dpal ldan 'bras spungs su rgyal ba lnga pa mjal zhing /
khong gi mdun nas 'jigs byed kyi dbang dang /
rta mgrin dang tshe dbang bcas zhus /
de nas mi ring bar gtsang bkra shis lhun por bskyod /
lam bar chos lugs ris med kyi dgon khag rnams su mjal skor mdzad /
bkra shis lhun por 'byor pa'i nyin par /
paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa mjal /
de'i phyi nyin bla ma dkon mchog rgyal mtshan mjal /
kun rig gi dbang sogs zhus /
khong gis bkra shis lhun po'i rgyud grwar sdod ces gsungs /
de nas rgyud pa grwa tshang du bzhugs rjes /
lha sar smon lam chen mor mjal bar phebs /
dge 'dun khri phrag la mang 'gyed phul /
lha sar gling sdod chos rje mdun sman bla'i rjes gnang bcas zhus /
phyi lo'i dpyid kar gtsang du yar log ste bkra shis lhun por rgyud pa grwa tshang du gsan sbyong mdzad /
dgung lo nyi shu par paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi drung nas bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa mnos /
de nas sog yul du log mdor na dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyi shu lhag bsten cing /
bka' lung dbang sogs shin tu mang po zhus /
rang yul du phebs rjes /
dgon gsar bkra shis dge 'phel gling du bzhugs /
bstan bcos 'ga' zhig rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i lcags mo lug gi lo la brtsams 'dug pas /
dgung grangs lnga bcu rtsa grangs la 'das sam snyam /

... rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sngags btu'i byin rlabs ji ltar bya ba'i tshul mchog mthun dngos grub kyi bang mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /

... kun rig gi bsnyen yig ngan 'gro'i mun pa sel ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub dkyil yo ga'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... skyabs mgon paN chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po'i zhabs brtan bdud sde'i gnyis 'thung 'joms pa'i gdong lnga'i sgra dbyangs dang rje rang nyid kyi zhabs brtan bcas bzhugs so / /
...  yongs 'dzin rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs brtan 'dod dgu'i 'byung gnas bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe rta zung 'brel gyi dbang bya tshul bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe dpag med lha gcig bum gcig tu grags pa'i tshe dbang bskur tshul bzhugs so / /
... bde mchog dkar po'i sgo nas tshe sgrub bya tshul 'gyur med rdo rje'i brag ri zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... bcom ldan 'das rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor sgrub cing mchod pa'i tshe /
bdag mdun gyi bzlas pa'i skabs dang mdun bskyed kyi gtso mo'i las bcol gyi dmigs pa ji ltar bya tshul dang /
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi ye shes 'beb sngags /
drug cu pa'i zor 'phen /
gtor ma brgya rtsa soD kyi skor la dri ba bkod pa'i lan chabs cig tu bkod pa bzhugs so / /

... bka' brgyad stong pa'i lung gi steng nas gsung bshad thob pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dang rtsa ba'i bla ma'i bka' drin gsol 'debs sogs bzhugs so / /

gu ge yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin ni /
gtsang g.yas ru bde rgyas bye ma gling gi gtsug lag khang dang nye ba /
chu bo lo ha ti'i nye 'dabs brgya mkhar zhes pa'i yul du /
yab tshe  ring dpal 'byor dang yum 'dzom chog gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gsum pa'i sa pho 'brug gi lo la 'khrungs /
byis pa btsas ma thag yab nas mtshan bkra shis don grub ces btags /
dgung lo dgu par phebs pa na /
kha ba blo bzang brtson 'grus mdun rab tu byung /
ming blo bzang bstan 'dzin gnang /
bkra shis lhun por chos spyod sogs kyi rgyugs legs par phul /
dgung lo bcu par mkhan chen ye shes rgyal mtshan mdun dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
tshogs chen ngag 'don gyi rim pa dang grwa tshang chos spyod rnams la sbyong brtson dang /
dkyil khang grwa tshang du tshad ma'i skor la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad pas dka' bcu'i ming btags bzhes /
slob dpon rin chen dge slong chos rje'i mdun sgra dang sdeb sbyor sbyangs /
dgung lo nyer brgyad par /
paN chen blo bzang dpal ldan ye shes drung nas dge slong gi sdom pa mnos /
de nas lo bcu bzhi tsam dpal 'byor lhun po'i ri khrod sogs gnas dben pa bsten nas nyams len mdzad cing /
rgyal ba'i gsung rab dgongs 'grel dang bcas par go ba mthar phyin par gyur /
dgung lo zhe lnga par dkyil 'khor grwa tshang gi slob dpon du gyur /
dgung lo zhe brgyad par rgyud pa grwa tshang gi slob dpon du bskos /
dgung lo zhe dgu par paN chen blo bzang bstan pa'i nyi ma'i yongs 'dzin du gyur /
de nas bzung gu ge yongs 'dzin zhis pa'i mtshan snyan thob /
khong gi gsung <'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang bshad> kyi mjug tu rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i shing mo phag la brtsams par 'khod tshul la btas na /
de dus khong dgung lo drug cu re brgyad du phebs yod pas sku tshe ring tsam bzhugs yod pa 'dra /
khong gi gsung rab ni nged dpe mdzod khang du ka nas ca'i bar po ti lnga bzhugs so / /

dgung lo drug cu re gnyis pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i chu lug lo la sku gshegs so /

... sems kyi dri ma 'byed pa'i tshul gser 'gyur rtsi'i dpes bstan pa bzhugs / /

'gro mgon gtsang pa rgya ras pa'i slob ma bu chen drug gi tha ma rgod tshang pa ni /
rab byung gsum pa'i sa mo bya'i lo la lho brag dol po chung du 'khrungs /
dgung lo gzhon dus nas bla ma'i bka' ltar /
lho brag 'khar chu dang /
gangs ti se /

dpal sa skya 'khon gyi gdung rgyud sngags 'chang shes rab rgyal mtshan ni /

mdo khams dang hor gyi yul gru 'ga' la'ang ldom bur phebs /
rab byung brgyad pa'i chu pho stag gi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bco lngar 'das /

rgya nag pa 'jam dbyangs bstan pa'i nyi ma'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka rje 'jam dbyangs bstan pa'i nyi ma'i rnam thar bka' rtsom mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... zab mo lta ba'i dmigs khrid thar ba'i sgo 'byed bzhugs so / /
...  dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i bstan bcos kyi 'grel ba mi pham dgongs zab gsal ba'i legs bshad sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lam rim chung ngu'i bden gnyis skabs kyi mchan 'grel blo bzang dgongs rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... shes khyad byed po'i mtshan nyid bzhi'i rnam bzhag yum don ku mud bzhad pa'i legs bshad zla zer snang ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bye smra'i 'dod tshul gyi dogs slong blo gsal dga' skyid bzhugs so / /
... dge 'dun nyi shu'i rnam bzhag gi tshig nyung go bde don gsal nor bu'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  phar phyin skabs kyi dris lan 'ga' bzhugs so / /
... blo sbyong don bdun ma'i zin bris rgyal sras 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... pan chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma phyogs las rnam rgyal dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas bslab bya'i tshul du gdams pa'i chab shog gi 'grel ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstod 'grel 'jam dbyangs dgyes pa'i mchod sprin mkha' 'gro rnam par rtsen pa'i rgyud mangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... dpal ldan rig pa 'dzin pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba sprin gyi zhon pa'i rtogs brjod mkha' 'gro rnam par rtsen ba'i rgyud mangs ngo mtshar rna ba'i bcud len zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgur 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
... lta mgur gyi 'grel pa mkhas pa dgyes pa'i mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mdo rgyud sogs 'don tshul bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor dngos grub nor bu'i gter mdzod zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje sems dpa' dang mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i tshogs mchod bzhugs so / /
...  dmigs brtse ma'i khongs su mdo sngags kyi lam yongs su rdzogs pa bsdus nas shar sgom byed tshul 'jam mgon bla ma mnyes byed kun bzang mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sgrol dkar tshe khrid 'chi med dngos grub stsol ba'i man ngag zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rdzogs rim gyi rnam bshad gsang chen sgo brgya 'byed pa'i lde mig zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i man ngag brjed byang du bkod pa 'jigs mdzad zhal lung snyan rgyud bdud rtsi'i thigs pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi bskyed rim bde chen 'dod 'jo bzhugs so / /
... dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i skor las brtsams pa'i dris lan legs bshad padmo'i ljon pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor khri bshad sogs thor bu 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
...  legs par bshad pa rigs ldan dgyes pa'i mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal phyag na rdo rje la brten pa'i 'chi med tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa bdud rtsi zil mngar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum chen gyi bsnyen sgrub man ngag snyan rgyud bdud rtsi'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa thugs rje chen po bcu gcig zhal gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub cing mchod pa'i rim pa  nag po 'gro shes su bkod pa 'phags mchog dgyes pa'i kun bzang mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rdo rje sems dpa' la brten nas stong mchod 'bul tshul gyi cho ga nyes ltung dri ma dag byed kun bzang mchod pa'i sprin phung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po yid bzhin nor bu'i gtor sgrub bya tshul chog bsgrigs 'dod pa kun ster bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras la brten nas nor dang tshe dpal bskyed pa'i cho ga 'dod dgu 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal ldan lha mo'i bzlog bsgyur bya tshul gnod 'tshe kun sel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal ldan srad rgyud lugs kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i khrid yig dngos grub gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /

'jam dbyangs bstan pa'i nyi ma ni /
rab byung bcu gcig pa'i me pho stag gi lo la hor gyi yul du 'khrungs /
dgung lo bdun par sde khri rin po che'i drung du rab byung bsgrubs te grwa btsun mdzad /
sbyor klog sogs sbyong ba'i mgo brtsams /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par /
bla ma 'jam dbyangs mdun du byams chos dang dbu ma rigs tshogs bcas kyi tshig rgyug phul /
rgyug bzang po byung bas legs so thob /
dgung lo bcu drug par /
blo rig dang rtags rigs sogs tshad ma'i skor gyi 'bel gtam mdzad /
de nas lo nyer lnga'i bar gzhung pod lngar sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad /
dgung lo nyer lnga par rje 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje'i bka' lung bzhin /
mdzod dang 'dul ba sogs kyi brgal lan byas /
mkhas pa'i grags pa thob /
khong ni sku tshe'i stod la bla brang du slob  gnyer mdzad cing /
de nas hor gyi yul du khal kha sogs su bzhugs pa dang skabs 'gar dkor rgyug kyang mdzad /
tshe mjug tsam la rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar phebs /
de phyir khong la rgya nag pa zhes pa'i ming thob /
khong nam 'das pa sogs rnam thar ma mjal bas kha tshon gcod thabs bral /
khong gi gsung ni <lta mgur gyi 'grel pa mkhas pa dgyes pa'i mchod sprin> sogs mgur dang snyan ngag chab shog dang gzhung 'grel /
dris lan dang rtogs brjod sogs bstan bcos sum cu so gsum yod pa de nyid po ti gnyis su byas nas bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du dpar brkos yod cing /
nged dpe mdzod khang du po ti gnyis po cha tshang bzhugs yod /

rgyal mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka ston pa mnyam med thub pa'i dbang po'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis mdor bsdus te brjod pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  mnyam med shA kya'i rgyal po dang 'dzam gling mdzes byed rgyan drug mchog gnyis kyi rtogs pa brjod pa lha'i dpag bsam ljon shing zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ngo bo rgyal ba blo bzang grags pa la gsol ba 'debs pa'i smon tshig bsam pa lhun gyis 'grub pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po rgyal mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan pa'i zhal snga nas kyi rnam par thar pa nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal sras lag len gyi 'grel pa gzhan phan bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel pa / /

... ga rdo rje 'chang chen por dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas la bstod cing gsol ba 'debs pa'i rab tu byed pa dngos grub kyi snye ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i khrid yig las tshogs dang bcas pa dngos grub kun 'byung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i khrid yig byin rlabs myur 'jug ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim dmar khrid dngos grub gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyud sde bzhi'i lha'i bsnyen pa byed tshul bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho dngos grub nor bu'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  thun drug gi rnal 'byor mdor bsdus dngos grub 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dril bu lha lnga'i dbang gi cho ga gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dpal rta mchog rol ba gsang bsgrub kyi dbang gi cho ga nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'jam dpal zhi khro dbyer med kyi zhi ba'i sbyin sreg byed tshul dngos grub kun 'byung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... khro bcu'i sbyin sreg dngos grub dpal 'bar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i mngon rtogs bzhugs so / /
... yum chen mo'i mngon rtogs zab lam gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i sgrub thabs 'chi med bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshogs bdag dmar po'i sgrub thabs bsam 'phel dbang rgyal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa dzam+b+hal dkar po'i bskang chog 'dod dgu'i char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu la brten pa'i g.yang 'bod bya tshul 'dod don 'dab brgya 'byed pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /

... dam can rdo rje legs pa'i sgo nas nor sgrub bya tshul gyi dgos don lag tu blang bde bsgrigs chog nor bu'i gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe ring mched lnga gtso bor gyur pa'i bod khams skyong ba'i gnas srung yul lha gzhi bdag rnams la phyogs gcig tu mchod gtor 'bul tshul lha bsrung dgyes pa'i rol mo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dgra lha mched dgu la mchod gtor 'bul tshul dang dgra lha'i dpangs bstod sogs byed tshul gyi cho ga dngos grub bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... grub pa'i slob dpon chen po mtsho skyes rdo rje'i sku brnyan mthong ba don ldan rten dang brten par bcas pa'i dkar chag mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi skor don gnyis lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /

... rje bla ma mtshan brjod par dka' ba dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me dpal bzang po'i rtogs pa brjod pa ngo mtshar lha'i rol mo mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /

... bstod tshogs kyi skor byin rlabs myur 'jug tshangs pa'i glu dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gsol 'debs kyi skor bden tshig lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgur ma'i bskor thar 'dod bung ba'i glu dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan la gnang ba'i bslab bya bzhugs so / /
... tsha gsur bsngo tshul gyi 'grel ba bde legs 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i bum chog bzhugs so / /
... thugs rje chen po'i bsgom bzlas dang skra chog sogs bzhugs so / /
...  zab lam gcod kyi rgyun 'khyer mkha' 'gro'i zhal lung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba'i bdag po la brten nas gza' klu'i dug dbyung bya tshul bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gza' mchog chen po la mchod gtor 'bul tshul 'dod don lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... skyes bu gsum gyi chos skyong la mchod gtor 'bul tshul dngos grub kun 'byung sogs gtor bsngos kyi rim pa bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba'i bstan srung chen mo ma cig grags mo rgyal gyi gsol mchod 'dod dgu'i gru char 'bebs pa'i rdzogs ldan sprin chen zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha chen tshangs pa chen po'i gtor chog dngos grub char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yul skyong gzhi bdag rnams kyi bsangs kyi cho ga dge legs char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... chab shog mtho ris dpal mo'i rna rgyan u t+pala phreng mdzes bzhugs so / /
... dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngo ba'i smon tshig gi rim pa byang chen bgrod pa'i them skas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... cha myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs sna tshogs skor  bzhugs so / /
... 'od dpag med la brten pa'i bzang spyod kyi sgo nas 'chi ba blu ba'i cho ga 'chi med grub pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sprul sku myur 'byon gyi skor phan bde'i nyi ma 'dren pa'i shing rta zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dul ba lung sde bzhi'i dka' gnad yongs su rdzogs par bsdus pa skal bzang re ba kun skong zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dul ba'i dka' gnad rnam par dpyad pa 'khrul spong blo gsal mgul rgyan tsit+ta ma Ni'i phreng mdzes skal bzang re ba kun bskong las gzhi smad bsdus pa bzhugs so / /
... su nyid dge bshes ngag dbang gi dris lan gya tshom gcod pa'i ral gri zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po'i rnam par thar pa dad pa'i padmo rgyas pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  rje mkhas grub 'phrin las dbang phyug gi rnam par thar pa mdo tsam brjod pa bdud rtsi'i rdzing bu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dran pa shes rab bkra shis kyi rnam thar mu thi la'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gser khang chen mo rten dang brten par bcas pa'i dkar chag byang chen thar lam bgrod pa'i them skas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  'byung ba bzhi'i sa ts+tsha 'debs tshul bzhugs so / /
... tshig bkra'i skor bzhugs so / /
... dmigs brtse ma'i 'khor lo 'bri tshul dge legs 'byung pa'i snye ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dkar chag dad pa'i sgo 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /

chos 'khor rgyal gyi mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan ni /
mdo smad lho rgyud kyi sa char 'bor zhes pa'i grong sde ru /
yab yum skyabs dang yum lha mo mtsho gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gsum pa'i chu pho rta'i lo la 'khrungs /
dgung grangs bdun par phebs pa na /
dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho'i drung du ka mad sbyor klog bcas sbyangs /
dgung lo bcu gcig par se ra dge bshes blo bzang chos 'phel mdun rab tu byung /
mtshan blo bzang don grub ces gsol /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du phebs /
gung thang rin po che dang lhan cig chos grwar zhugs /
dgung lo bcu drug par rje bsod nams dbang rgyal mdun nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
skabs der 'jam bzhad dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang pos khong sgo mang bla ma sangs rgyas rdo rje'i yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad de khrir bkod /
lha zhis dka' bcu pa dang kha gya dar rgyas gnyis slob dpon du brten /
gzhung pod yongs la go rim ldan par gsan sbyong mdzad /
dgung lo nyer  gcig par rje 'jam bzhad mdun nas dge slong gi sdom pa blangs /
mtshan grags pa rgyal mtshan zhes btags /
dge bshes blo bzang 'jigs med mdun snyan ngag sbyangs /
dgung lo nyer gnyis pa chu mo yos kyi lo'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes drug la dbus su phebs nas zla ba dgu par lha ldan du 'byor /
gtsug lag khang dang dgon gnas yongs la gnas mjal phebs shing khyad par rtse po ta lar tA la'i brgyad pa 'jam dpal rgya mtsho mjal /
de nas 'bras sgo mang grwa tshang du grwa sar zhugs /
hor skal bzang don grub dang gung thang rin po che gnyis dge rgan du bsten /
dgung lo nyer lnga par 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dbus su phebs pa dang lhan du /
dga' ldan dgon sogs mjal ba brgyud gtsang du phebs /
bkra shis lhun por paN chen blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma mjal /
de nas slar 'bras sgo mang du tshur log ste slob gnyer mdzad /
skabs der 'jam dbyangs bzhad pas khong rgyal gyi gdan sar bsko bzhag gi bka' gnang ba'i rkyen gyis /
sde pa gzhung nas bka' byung bar brten /
chos 'khor rgyal gyi gdan khrir phebs /
der yun ring ma 'gor bar 'ol kha sogs brgyud de sgo mang du tshur log gzhung pod lnga la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad /
sgo mang grwa tshang gi tshogs dbus su gzhung pod lnga'i dam bca' bzhag khyad par smon lam chen mor gdan sa gsum gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen sum stong lhag gis gtsos dge 'dun khri phrag zung brgal ba'i dbus su dam pa'i chos kyi 'bel gtam seng ge'i nga ro bsgrags /
log smra wa skyes tshogs dag ming med du bcom /
sde pa gzhung nas dam bca' ang dang thob pa'i rtags mtshon na bza' sogs srol ltar gnang bar ma tshad dge bshes lha rams pa'i mtshan snyan phul /
dgung lo nyer bdun pa sa pho sprel gyi lor /
'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang pos mgron gnyen rab 'byams pa blo bzang tshul khrims ngo g.yog khong gdan 'dren du dbus su mngags pa dang lhan cig byang lam brgyud de zla ba brgyad par bla brang du 'byor /
chibs bsu ser sbreng dang bcas bkra shis 'khyil du bsus /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pas khong bla brang mkhan por bskos /
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi bya ba dang dgon par rten gsar bzhengs /
dge 'dun par mang 'gyed sogs legs par bsgrubs /
dgung lo sum cu bzhes pa lcags mo phag gi lor rje 'jigs med dbang pos rang nyid kyi rgyun du spyod rgyu'i thub sku gser zangs ma dang /

chu tshags /
las chog gi dpe cha rnams khong la gnang zhing /
de mtshungs su nged bsdad med dus gzhung gi don che phra tshang ma nged sgug sdod mi dgos mkhan po zhabs drung la zhus nas thag bcad na chog ces dril bsgrags /
de nas bzung bkra shis 'khyil gyi chos dang 'jig rten gyi bya ba yongs kyi 'gan 'khur bzhes /
lo de'i zla ba bcu par khong rgan gya'i phyogs su 'bul sdud la phebs pa'i lam bar 'jam bzhad gshegs pa'i gtam ngan gsan /
tshes nyer dgu la  bla brang du rje'i sku gdung mjal /

'bul sdud ched mtsho sngon por phebs /
lo gnyis tsam 'gor /

byams sku lha khang dang bcas pa legs par grub ste rab gnas mdzad /
dgung lo bzhi bcu par bla brang tshogs chen gyi gdan khrir phebs /
dgung lo zhe gsum par khri 'dzin dgongs pa zhus te 'jam bzhad yang srid tshogs dbus su gdan drangs /
phyi lo nas bzung dben gnas bkra shis dge 'phel du phebs sku mtshams bcad /
lo lnga drug tsam gyi dus su /
lha 'bangs kha gya dang /
dngul ra sde tsho gnyis kyi bar 'khrug rtsod byung /
sku mtshams grol nas bar sdum la byon /
de nas yang tshogs chen gyi gdan khrir 'khod /
mdor na khong gi sku tshe hril por tshogs chen gdan khrir lan gsum phebs te chos srid kyi bya ba legs par bsgrubs /
sku tshe'i 'jug tu sgrub pa nyams len kho nar 'bad de dus 'da' bar mdzad /
rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i me pho spre'u'i lo yar mar tsam la sku gshegs pa yin no /

... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /

tsong kha pa'i slob ma gtso bo dka' bcu pa rgyal tshab dar ma rin chen ni /
gtsang nyang stod kyi yul du rab byung drug pa'i shing pho 'brug gi lo la sku bltams /
gnas rnying pa rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi drung nas rab tu byung /
dka' bzhi pa ring rdor sogs slob dpon du bsten nas dam chos mang du gsan /
sa skya'i red mda' ba gtsos mkhas chen du mar bsten nas /
mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs kun la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad /
sa skya dang gsang phu /
rtse thang bcas su po ti dka' ba bcu'i grwa skor gnang /
rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan dang /
mkhas chen g.yag pa sogs sa skya'i mkhas chen rnams dang rtsod gleng legs par mdzad de mkhas pa'i grags pa thob cing /
dka' bcu pa'i ming rtags blangs /
de nas mi ring bar tsong kha pa'i slob ma gtso bor gyur /
khong dgung lo nga drug tu phebs pa sa mo phag gi lo la tsong kha pa 'das nas /
tsong kha pa'i tshab tu dga' ldan gser khrir bzhugs /
de nas bzung khong la rgyal tshab ces pa'i ming thob /
gdan sa lo bcu gcig 'dzin cing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi bya ba kho na mdzad /
de nas mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang gdan sar bkod de zur bzhugs mdzad /
dgung lo re dgu pa rab byung bdun pa'i chu pho byi ba'i lo zla ba lnga par rtso po ta lar sku gshegs /
khong ni tsong kha pa las lo bdun gyis gzhon la /
tsong kha pa 'das rjes lo bcu gsum bzhugs /
mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang ni khong las lo nyer gcig gis gzhon no /
khong gi gsung ni dbu ma rtsa ba shes rab dang 'jug pa sogs dbu ma'i rnam bshad dang /
tshad ma'i skor gyi bshad pa /
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa sogs gsang sngags kyi skor bcas po ti ka pa nas nya pa'i bar brgyad nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod /
...  ...ka...nya...  @# / /
rgyal rong dge bshes tshul khrims nyi ma'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... rje thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i rten 'brel bstod pa legs bshad snying po'i rnam bshad yid kyi mun sel shes rab sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... theg pa chen po'i blo sbyong gi shar sgom myong 'khris ma'i brjed byang dran pa gso ba'i bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam gyi tshig don rab tu gsal bar byed pa'i sgron gsal bzhugs so / /
... dben sa snyan rgyud kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor thun mong ma yin pa dang 'brel ba'i phyag chen gyi 'khrid man ngag zhal shes dang bcas pa'i kha chems rlung la bskur ba'i 'phrin yig bzhugs so / /
... bslab sbyong gnyis sbyar ba'i lam bsgrigs grub pa'i mig sman zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sa rgyan lam sgrigs mu tig phreng ba rang gi rnam par dpyod pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... skyes tshoms sbyar ba'i lam bsgrigs nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  @# / /
rgyal sras skal bzang thub bstan gyi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka rgyal sras rin po che'i gsung 'bum dkar chag /
... skyabs mgon rigs brgya'i khyab bdag thub dbang rdo rje 'chang dang dbyer ma mchis pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan ye shes dpal bzang pos byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i dmar khrid thams cad mkhyen par bgrod pa'i bde lam myong khrid du mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... byang chub kyi sems sbyong ba'i man ngag dang bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rim gnyis chos rgyal rigs ldan 'byung tshul bstan pa'i gnas tshad dri med 'od kyi bsdus don bcas phyogs gcig tu bkod pa legs bshad gsal ba'i sgron me bzhugs so / /
... lam khrid bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhabs brtan gsol 'debs smon tshig rnams phyogs gcig tu sgrigs pa phan bde'i re skong bzhugs so / /
... yi dam rgyud sde'i lha tshogs rnams kyi sgrubs thabs dbang rjes gnang tshe sgrub rab gnas sbyin sreg yul khrus bsangs mchod sogs kyi rim pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bkod pa bde chen 'dod dgu'i char 'bebs bzhugs so / /
... rtsis kyi bstan bcos nyin byed snang ba'i rgyan mchog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  gtsug lag rtsis kyi skor 'go gson rtsis rde'u zhe bdun gyi gsal byed blo gsal dga' byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sdeb sbyor dang daN+Ti'i gzhung las le'u gnyis pa'i dper brjod dang gsum pa'i kun bzang 'khor lo 'tsho byed sman gyi bshad pa dbyangs 'char lung bstan gsal ba'i sgron me rnams bzhugs so / /
... tshe chog 'dod 'jo dbang gi rgyal po'i sa'i cho ga dgongs don rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... kha dkar chag /
... skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang rgyal sras bskal bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtshos dpal rdo rje phreng ba'i bka' dbang gnang ba'i zin bris bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa thugs rje chen po dpal mo lugs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ngag 'don bde legs kun 'byung gi dgongs pa rab gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mi tra brgya rtsa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs rnams kyi mngon par rtogs pa mu tig phreng ba'i gsal byed blo gsal mgul rgyan bzhugs so / /
... dpal dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rim pa dang po'i rnam bshad pad dkar zhal lung dngos grub bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang gi rnam bshad dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba'i 'od rgyan zhes  bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun mi pham mgon po'i dbu thog gi rgya phubs gsasr bzhengs dkar chag dang /
bca' yig chos bsrungs rnams la mchod gtor 'bul tshul 'phrin bcol snyan shal thang sku mchod rdzas sogs kyi smon tshig rin chen mchod pa'i sprin phung bzhugs so / /
rab gnas dge legs char 'bebs kyi ngag 'don bkra shis bdud rtsi'i char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba'i bdag po 'khor lo chen po'i rim gnyis kyi rnam bshad gsang chen myur lam sogs bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... ga byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i sa bcad bzhugs so / /
... lam rim gyi myong khrid skal ldan thar 'dod 'jug ngogs bzhugs so / /
... byang chub lam gyi rim pa bde lam gyi myong khrid dben sa snyan rgyud kyi man ngag gi brgyan pa bla ma dam pa'i zhal shes dngos grub gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che gser sbyangs btso mas gsar bzhengs kyi dkar chag dge legs 'dod dgu char du snyil ba dpag bsam yongs 'du'i 'khri shing zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i bla rgyud dang bdag skyed bcas kyi cho ga'i ngag 'don 'dod pa 'jo pa'i bum bzang bzhugs so / /
...  dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i bum bskyed dang mdun bskyed sgrub cing mchod pa 'dod 'jo'i ngag 'don khrigs chags su bkod pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i dbang chog smon lam shis brjod 'dod pa 'jo ba'i ngag 'don khrigs chags su bkod pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i sa chog sta gon gyi rim pa 'dod pa 'jo ba'i ngag 'don khrigs chags su bkod pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga'i ngag 'don khrigs chags su bkod pa 'dod pa 'jo ba'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha bcu gsum gyi sgrub dkyil ngag 'don ngan song sdug bsngal sel ba'i rtsi sman zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gsung thor bu'i gras srad rgyud lugs kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs bla ma'i rnal 'byor skor bzhugs / /
... gsung thor bu las yi dam sgrub skor mkha' spyod ma'i sbyin sreg sogs bzhugs / /
... gsung thor bu las 'jigs byed sogs kyi rim gnyis kyi khrid dang gtum mo khrid bcas bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i lag mchod bde chen gsal ba ngag 'don du bsgrigs pa dge legs 'dod dgu char 'bebs dang gsang 'dus dang mgon po'i tshogs 'khor sogs bzhugs so / /
...  sdom gsum so so'i bsngo bgrang bshags sdom bya tshul bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun nyin zhag phrug gcig gi kun sbyong bcas bzhugs so / /
... 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs zhabs brtan snyan dar 'dod gsol yang srid myur 'byon sogs thor bya rnams bzhugs so / /
... bstan bsrung chen po rdo rje legs pa'i gsol mchod 'phrin las rnam bzhi lhun grub zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... @# /
rgyal sras bskal bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho ni rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i chu mo phag gi lo la 'khrungs /
pan chen dpal ldan ye shes dang /
lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje sogs mkhas chen mang po slob dpon du bsten /
snyan ngag dang sum rtags /
nang don rig pa'i skor gyi mdo dang sngags kyi gzhung mang por gsan sbyong mdzad cing /
khyad par gsang sngags la mkhas pa chen por gyur /
khong gi mtshan la yongs 'dzin no min han yang zer /
khong gi gsung rab ni /
dbang bskur rjes gnang dang /
rab gnas /
snyan ngag gi dpe brjod sogs mang du yod pa rnams po ti gsum du bsdus pa dge ldan par ma cha tshang nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod /
...  @# / /
rgyal sras thogs med bzang po'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... rgyal ba'i sras po thogs med chen po'i bka' 'bum bzhugs so / /
... bris ma /
... rgyas sras rin po che'i bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag ma rig mun sel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gdams ngag gi skor bzhugs so / /
... rgyal sras rin po che'i rnam thar rgyas pa bzhugs / /
... phyag 'tshal bstod pa'i skor bzhugs / /
... sems bskyed /
chos spyod /
cho ga dang bsgom bzlas /
gtor 'bul sogs bzhugs / /
... zhal gdams thor bu ba'i skor / /
... rten 'brel snying po'i 'khrid yig dang skyid sdug lam khyer bzhugs / /
... snying po don gsum gyi don bsdus bzhugs / /
...  rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... @# /
rgyal sras thogs med bzang po ni /
gtsang sa skya dgon pa'i lhor dpag tshad phyed gsum tsam gyi sar brag skya zhes pa'i yul du /
yab dkon mchog dpal dang /
yum 'bum sgron gnyis las rab byung lnga pa'i shing mo lug gi lo la 'khrungs /
dgung lo gsum par yum 'das /
dgung lo lnga par yab gshegs /
dgung lo bcu bzhir phebs pa sa pho sprel lo'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes brgyad nyin gyi snga dror /
bsam gling pa'i gdung rgyud bla ma dpal 'bar nas mkhan po dang /
de'i gcung po mkhan po rin chen dpal bzang nas slob dpon mdzad pa'i mdun /
rab tu byung zhing dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
ming bzang po dpal btags /
dgung lo bco lnga par /
bo dong e waM gling gi chos grwa chen mor byon /
bla ma kun rgyal pa'i drung du mngon pa sbyangs /
sa skya dgon par phebs bla ma gzhon rgyal mdun tshad ma sde bdun sogs tshad ma'i skor rnams gsan /
dgung lo nyer gsum par gtsang phyogs kyi chos grwa yongs la grwa skor mdzad /
tshad ma'i rtsod pa 'gran zla dang bral bas kun gyis bsngags brjod byas /
dgung lo sum cu par /
byang sems rin chen mgon gyi mdun nas bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blangs /
dgung lo so dgu par /
'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan sogs nas nan gyi bskul ba dang du blangs te chos grwa chen po bo dong e d+ha ra'i gdan sa mdzad /
dgung lo zhe gsum par dngul chu chos rdzong du mtshams lo nyi shu lhag bzhugs /
rang byung drug pa'i sa mo bya'i lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyi shu nyin gyi phyi dror nyi ma nub pa dang mnyam du sku gshegs /
khong dgung grangs don lnga bzhugs /
khong gi slob ma ni mkhan chen byang chub rtse mo dang /
chos rje nyi ma gzhon nu sogs /
mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i slob ma shin tu mang ngo /
khong gi gsung ni /
nged dpe mdzod khang du par ma po ti gcig dang /
bris ma pod 'ga' yod /
...  @# / /
rgyal sras blo bzang ngag dbang thogs med kyi gsung 'bum / /
... bris ma /
... rgyal sras rdo rje 'chang gi gsung 'bum dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... skyabs 'khrid sa bcad bzhugs so / /
... skyabs 'khrid bzhugs so / /
... skyabs 'khrid rgyal bstan rin po che'i sgo 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... byang chub bde lam gyi bshad pa'i zin bris ngo mtshar legs bshad zla tshes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... skyabs 'gro'i 'khrid yig rgyal bstan rin po che'i sgo 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bsnyen rdzogs paN chen sdom rgyun gyi brgyud 'debs sogs bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
