rgyal sras blo bzang ngag dbang thogs med ni /
dus rabs bcu dgu pa'i smad tsam gyi mi  yin zhing /
mtshan la blo bzang ngag dbang thogs med bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho yang zer /
khong ni mdo smad phyogs kyi dgon pa zhig gi sprul sku yin nam snyam par dpyad /
khong gi gsung ni /
skyabs khrid sa bcad dang /
skyabs khrid sogs sne grangs dgu po ti gcig tu bsdus pa dbu can bris ma zhig nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod /
...  @# / /
rgyal sras yon tan 'od kyi gsung 'bum / /
... bris ma /
... rgyal sras yon tan 'od kyi bka' 'bum thor bu las gsol 'debs dang /
bstod pa /
smon lam bcas bzhugs / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... @# /
rgyal sras yon tan 'od ni /
spyi lo'i dus rabs bcu bzhi pa'i smad tsam gyi mi yin zhing /
sa skya bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang blo gros shes rab sogs slob dpon du bsten nas dam pa'i chos mang du gsan /
dgung nar son pa na dngul chu chos rdzong du yun ring ma bzhugs par gnas nges med du phebs te bya bral ba mdzad /
khong gi bla ma bso nams rgyal mtshan ni /
sa skya bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal gyi sras tha chung yin la /
tsong kha pa la'ang dbang gnang myong ba red /
khong gi gsung ni /
ldeb 'bring nag bris ma shog ldeb bzhi brgya dang dgu yod pa'i po ti gcig nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod cing /
tshig tshang ma mgur ma tshigs su bcad pa sha stag yin no /
...  @# / /
sgo mang blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtsho'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka 'jam mgon rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'dzin skyong sbel ba la 'gran zla dang bral ba sgo mang mkhan blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtsho ba'i rnam par thar ba thar 'dod lam bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  rnam thar gsol 'debs dad gus 'dab brgya bzhad pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun bla ma dang rtsa ba'i bla ma dbyer med du gsol ba 'debs pa don gnyis yid bzhin 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gnas lnga rig pa'i paN+Di ta chen po ko shri ngag dbang skal bzang ba'i 'khrungs rabs rnam thar g.yas 'khyil dung gi sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gsung thor bu'i skor bzhugs so / /
... rje blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gsung thor bu'i skor bzhugs so / /
... lam yongs su rdzogs pa'i smon tshig gi bsdus don rin chen mdzod kyi lde mig ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  yang sprul myur byon sogs kyi skor bzhugs so / /
... rje bla ma rgyan drug mchog gnyis dang bcas pa la phyag mchod 'bul ba'i tshul lag tu blang bde bar bkod pa byin rlabs nyin byed 'dren pa'i shing rta zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gsung 'gur dang chab shog skor bzhugs so / /
... sad bsrung gi 'don 'grig nag 'gros su bkod pa bzhugs so / /
...  sgron gsal gyi bsdus don bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba 'dus ba'i rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... 'jam mgon bla ma tsong kha pa chen po la brten nas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg ji ltar bya ba'i cho ga dngos grub kun 'byung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... grub chen dril bu zhabs kyi 'khor lo sdom pa lus dkyil kyi sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa bde chen snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa la brten pa'i khro bcu'i srung 'khor bsgom tshul gyi ngag 'don rgyas par bkod pa bgegs 'joms mtshon cha'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lus dkyil gyi rnal 'byor dang 'brel bar dbang bzhi thun mong ba dang thun mong ma yin pa stabs gcig tu len tshul mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
...  dpal 'khor lo sdom pa la brten nas phreng mo 'debs tshul kun gsal nor bu'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa la brten nas rmi lam brtag pa'i gdams pa nyin mor byed pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... kha zhi ba lam zab kyi don 'grel dmigs khrid kyi tshul du bkod pa gnad don kun gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ma cig mkha' 'gro snyan rgyud kyi phyi mtshams chen mor 'gro tshul gsal bar byed pa'i yi ge ngang pa'i mchu sgros zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ma cig khros ma nag mo lha lnga'i sgrub thabs kyi tshig don rnam par bshad pa mkha' 'gro'i dgongs rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po lha bcu gsum ma la brten pa'i bsam gtan gyi bdag 'jug ji ltar bya ba'i tshul gsal bar bkod pa dngos grub nor bu'i bang mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... shin tu gsang ba'i mgur dbyangs kyi 'grel pa rdo rje'i tshig gi mdud grol ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bde gsang 'jigs gsum gyi gzhal yas khang gi rnam bzhag mdor bsdus / /
...  zhwa ser bstan pa'i srog shing dam pa kirti mchog sprul rin po che nas dus 'khor gyi skor las brtsams te dri ba 'ga' zhig gnang ba'i lan sogs dris lan 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
... thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug dang bcas pa la phyag mchod thugs dam bskul ba'i tshul mdor bsdus te brjod pa phan bde'i char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mchod rten dkar chag rin chen gter gyi kha byang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i thugs rje bskul ba'i gsol 'debs dpyid kyi pho nya'i klu dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... khri bshad bzhugs / /
... seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma bla med lugs la brten nas tshogs 'khor bya tshul bzhugs so / /
... rgyal yum rje btsun ma sgrol ma la brten nas smyung bar gnas pa'i cho ga thar par bgrod pa'i them skas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun sgrol ma'i g.yang 'bod don gnyis mchog stsol zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal yum bcom ldan 'das seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma la brten nas tshe bsod dge mtshan spel ba'i cho ga 'dod dgu'i char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i mngon rtogs lag tu blang bde bar bkod pa tshe dpal bdud rtsi'i char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rgyas ba'i sbyin sreg bya tshul dngos grub 'dab  brgya bzhad pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sdom gsum gyi bslab bya go sla ba'i rtsom 'phro / /
... dzam dkar gter sgrub mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... bshad sgrub bstan pa'i dga' tshal dmu dge bkra shis 'khor lo'i mgon du bzhugs pa'i blo gsal don gnyer pa rnams kyi rtsod grwa'i 'gro tshul zhib par brjod pa pad dkar phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... glag tshang sgom grwar grags pa'i bca' yig blang dor gsal pa'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshad ma rnam 'grel le'u gnyis pa'i bsdus don zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba'i bstan srung gtso bo rnams la mchod gtor 'bul ba'i rim pa 'phrin las 'gugs ba'i lcags kyu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  bslab bya blang dor gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... @# /
sgo mang blo bzang tshul khrims ni /
rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i lcags mo glang gi lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu bdun nyin par /
mdo smad gling dkar stod kyi yod dar zhes pa'i yul du 'khrungs /
khong gi yab la chos shul yar 'phel dang /
yum la dpal shul dkon mchog skyid zer /
dgung lo gsum bzhes pa na /
paN chen dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi mas /
sgo mang chos dar gyi yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad /
dgung lo drug pa'i thog tig gya dkon mchog klog gi  slob dpon du bsten nas /
nga ro dang sbyor klog legs par sbyangs /
dgung lo bdun par phebs pa na /
bla brang bkra shis 'khyil nas gdan 'dren pa 'byor ba dang lhan cig tu bla brang dgon du phebs /
dga' bsu dang mdzad sgo gzab rgyas dang bcas sku gong ma'i bzhugs khrir mnga' gsol bar mdzad cing /
skya ser yongs nas 'bul ba gya nom pa phul /
lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig par /
'jam bzhad sku thog gsum pa blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtshos /
dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa stabs gcig tu gnang /
dge bshes dngul ra'i bsam gtan rgya mtsho slob dpon du bsten nas /
dge tshul gyi bslab bya bcu sogs gsan te yon tan gyi gzhi legs par btsugs /
skabs der bla brang du lo gcig lhag tsam bzhugs rjes rang yul du log yab chos shul dang gdan khri rin po che /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan sogs kyi mdun bka' chos mang du zhus /
khyad par dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis bka' bkod mdzad 'og blo 'dzin dang 'don rta dbyangs sogs la thogs pa med par gyur /
lo bzhi tsam rang yul bzhugs ring /
dus phal che ba dpal mang rin po che dang gur chung gcig gi nang bzhugs nas gsan sbyong mdzad /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par slar yang bla brang du phebs /
dgung lo bcu gsum par bla brang thos bsam gling gi chos grwar zhugs /
skabs der 'tsho ba ngan ngon la bsten cing /
brtson pa chen pos mdo sngags kyi gzhung lugs rnams dang /
rig gnas che phra kun la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad de /
gsung chos kyang 'ga' zhig brtsams /
de nas dgung lo nyer drug pa me stag lo'i zla ba lnga par dbus gtsang du phebs /
ta la'i dang paN chen gnyis la chos 'brel zhus /
dbus gtsang gi gtsug lag khang dang rten khyad 'phags yongs la phyag mchod dang /
gnas chen rnams su 'jam skor phebs /
zhar la dgon sde rnams su dpe cha dgos rigs dpar ba dang /
blu ba bcas mdzad de po ti brgya phrag tsam dos bsgril nas mar gdan rgyu mdzad /
dbus gtsang du lo bzhi tsam 'gor rjes /
dgung grangs nyer dgu pa sa sbrul lor r+wa rgya'i phyag mdzod sogs mi grangs bco brgyad lhan cig tu rim gyis rang yul du log lo de'i zla ba brgyad par bla brang du 'byor /
dgon sde tshang mas 'bul nor gya nom pa bstar /
khong gis khri bshad sogs mkhas pa mgu ba'i gsung bshad rgya cher mdzad /
gdan sa 'dzin pa'i dus su sog yul gyi yul gru rnams dang /
mdo smad kyi dgon gnas che phra yongs la zhabs kyis bcags te dam pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa tshad med bstsal /
mthar lcang skya ye shes bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis khong dgon lung du gdan nas rab byung bco lnga pa'i me mo lug gi lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes nyer lnga la dgon lung dgon par sku gshegs rjes sku gdung bla brang du gdan 'dren byas /
skabs der khong dgung grangs drug cu re bdun du phebs so /
khong gi gsung ni /

'bring 'tshams kyi cog ro'i rigs rgyud yin la /
sngon yab mes rnams 'bring 'tshams nas sa skya'i phyogs su gnas spos te 'brog las bsgrubs nas bzhugs pas /
phyis su sa skya bdag chen bzhi thog pa'i gsol ja par gyur /
de nas rim bzhin sa skya'i nye gnas chen po dpon tshang zhes grags shing /
khong gi yab ni dpon tshang grub pa yon tan dang /
yum ni bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i dpon seng gi sras mo bsod nams dpal ldan zhes pa de yin zhing rab byung drug pa'i chu pho khyi'i lo la dpal sa skyar sku bltams so /
dgung lo lnga par phebs pa na /
yab kyis rang re gsol ja ba'i rigs yin pas dngul gyi ja bo theg min lta dgos zhes ja bo dang ljid mnyam pa'i rdo ba  bkur nas 'byon bzhud mdzad bcug pas mi dgyes pa'i nyams kyis rdo ba sar 'phangs /
'jig rten pa'i bya ba la thugs mi dgyes pa'i tshul bstan /

de nas rim bzhin chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan mdun nas dge slong dang /
byang sems /
gsang ba sngags kyi sdom pa blangs /
mdo sngags kyi chos ma lus pa thugs la btags /
khyad par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i lugs kyi dkyil chog dang /
sgrub thabs rnams legs par gsan /
mkhas pa'i gras su tshud cing chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi sras kyi thu bor gyur /
dgung lo nyer lngar son pa na rje ye shes rgyal mtshan sku gshegs /
dgongs rdzogs kyi bya ba rnams legs par grub nas shangs chos 'khor sgang du byon /
lo ts+tsha ba skyabs mchog pa'i mdun na chos gsan /
de bzhin du zhe dgon du phebs nas bu d+hA shri'i mdun chos gsan /
khyad par sa bzang dgon par byon te sa bzang bla ma gzhon nu blo gros bla mar bsten nas dam chos yun ring gsan mthar /
khong dgung lo nyer dgur phebs pa rab byung bdun pa'i lcags pho stag gi lo la bla ma gzhon nu blo gros kyis /
nged yun ring e sdod mi shes /
khyod rang sa bzang dgon pa'i bdag po gyis la dgon sde legs par skyongs gsungs nas /
kri ya sa mu tsa'i glegs bam dang /
rdor dril /
chos dung rnams gnang nas rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol /
dgung lo nyer brgyad nas zhe dgu bar lo bcu dgu'i ring gdan sar bzhugs te dbyar dgun gnyis la bshad khrid dang /
ston dpyid gnyis la dbang lung dang sdom pa 'bogs pa sogs mdzad /
dbus gtsang khams gsum du khong la dge tshul slong gi sdom pa zhu mkhan khri phrag brgal ba byung zhing /
dbang dang khrid lung zhu mkhan ni de bas kyang mang /
dgung lo zhe dgu pa la gdan sar grwa pa mang zhing /
'jig rten gyi bya ba sogs g.yeng ba'i rgyu mang bas /
dben gnas shig tu phebs nas 'chad nyan mdzad na legs 'dug dgongs nas /
na bza' phug ri khrod dang /
bsam gling ri khrod sogs la thugs 'dun mdzad kyang brtags pa ma byung bas /
mthar e waM ri khrod du phebs /
der 'chad nyan sogs kyi bya ba shin tu 'phel bar brten /
phyag rdzas kyang rgya chen byung ba des /
gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs dang /
nang rten thub sku chen mo gser zangs las grub pa bal bo'i lha bzo a khe ra NA sogs bal bo'i lha bzos bzhengs pa dang /
gser btsos mas bzhengs pa'i bka' 'gyur sogs sku gsung thugs rten mang po gsar bzhengs mdzad cing /
bshad grwa btsugs pa sogs byas nas e waM chos  ldan gyi gdan sa chen po gsar tu spel /
slob ma'ang /
sa skya'i gdung rgyud bzhi thog pa kun dga' dbang phyug bdag chen chu mig pa blo gros dbang phyug ngor mkhan po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
gzhon nu rgyal mtshan dang dbang phyug grags bzang sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po du ma spel /
mnga' ris dang yar langs bcas la yang phebs te chos kyi sbyin pa bstsal /
khong dbang chen gnang skabs zang zing med pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa bstsal bas zhu mkhan lhag par mang /
khong ni dgung lo bco lnga nas bdun cu don lnga'i bar 'tsho ba ngan ngon la bsten cing sha spangs pa dang thos bsam dang 'chad nyan sogs la dka' ba tshad med spyad stabs sku lus thang po med cing bad kan skya rbab kyi nad yod pa'i rkyen gyis rgyun du sku gzugs la shed med pa dang sku sha rid pa zhig yin pas /
dgung lo don lngar phebs pa rab byung brgyad pa'i me pho byi ba'i lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes pa nyer gsum nyin thugs sras dkon mchog rgyal mtshan la /
sa paN gyi sku thang dang rgya'i rdor dril /
bla gos bcas gnang nas zhal ta mang po mdzad /
tshes nyer lnga'i snga dror nyi ma dros tsam la sku yi bkod pa chos dbyings su bsdus so /
khong gi gsung ni /
sgrub thabs skor dang /
thob yig cho ga rnam thar /
spring yig bcas dang po ti so so'i dkar chag rnams brtsis pas sna kha nyer gcig po po ti bzhi ru bsdus nas sde dger shing par brkos yod cing /
mtshan la e waM bka' 'bum zhes btags pa'i po ti bzhi po nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod /

... par ma /
... ka dpal 'khor lo'i dbang phyug 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po dkon mchog 'phel la bstod pa sgra rgyan me tog dkar po'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha dang bcas pa'i 'gro pa mtha' yas pa'i gtsug gi nor bu'i khri la zhabs zung gis rnam par brtsen pa'i 'dren mchog chos kyi rje'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba'i nyin byed bzhugs so / /
...  dpal sa skya lo tsA ba chen po'i rnam par thar pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi yon tan rnam par bkod pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos thos ba'i tshul gsal bar bshad pa'i yi ge thub bstan rgyas pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba'i legs par bshad pa bzhugs / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa'i nyams len bzhugs so / /
... bstan bcos rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi bsdus don tshang bde nyung gsal bzhugs so / /
... brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed bzhugs pa ngo mtshar che par snang ngo / /
... dpal kye rdo rje'i man ngag lugs kyi slob ma rjes su 'dzin pa'i tshul bzhugs so / /
...  kye rdo rje'i sa chog mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... bde mchog dpa' bo drug gi sgrub thabs byin rlabs kyi cho ga dang bcas pa bi ha ra tisma / /
... rdo rje lha mo'i bzlas pa sgom la brten nas 'chi med kyi dngos grub sgrub pa'i gdams ngag bzhugs so / /
... dpal ldan gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i / /
sgrub thabs bdud rtsi'i bum pa dang / /
dkyil chog bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun gyi / /

... ngag 'don phal cher ltos pa'i lha bcu gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig bzhugs so / /
... bya spyod spyi'i thig tshon gyi cho ga bzhugs so / /
... dpal ldan dges pa rdo rje yi / /

lugs mchog thun mong min pa bzhugs / /
... bris ma /
... dpal chos kyi rgyal po dkon mchog 'phel la bstod pa sgra rgyan me tog dkar po'i phreng ba bzhugs so / /
... rje bla ma 'dren mchog la bstod pa dngos grub kun 'byung bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun chos kyi rje sangs rgyas rin chen dpal bzang po la bstod pa bzhugs so / /
... mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal  bzang po la bstod pa ngo mtshar me tog gi phreng ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal sa skya lo tsa ba la gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i snye ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod bzhugs so / /
... rtsa ba'i bla ma rnam gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa snying gi thig le bzhugs so / /
... rtsa ba'i bla ma rnam gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i gsol 'debs bzhugs so / /
... mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa la phul ba / /
... bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phul ba'i zhu yig /
... yul khyad par can la mchod par brjod pa ngag gi 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... phud mchod dgos 'dod kun 'byung bzhugs so / /
... rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sku'i rnam 'gyur drug la nang gi rnam dag dang mthun par bstod pa / /
... byams pa mgon po la rnam thar dang mthun par bstod cing byams chos kyi lam rim rgyud la skye bar gsol ba 'debs pa ma pham dgongs rgyan bzhugs so / /
... 'dir ni dpal ldan sa skya yi /
'jam pa'i dbyangs la rab bsngags pa /
yon tan me  tog phur ma ste /
blo gsal mig gi bdud rtsi'o / /
... dbyangs can lha mo la bsngags pa /
don rgyan rnam par bkod pa yi /
phreng ba zhes bya blo gsal gyi /
dad pa'i mgrin pa mdzes byed do / /
... sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kyi kha rgyan bzhugs so / /
...  sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i brtsis nyung ngu rab gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i brtsis mkhas pa'i kha rgyan bzhugs so / /
... dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi /
bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam gyi mchog zab mo bla ma'i rnam thar gyi /
nyams len gsang ba'i nye lam bzhugs / /
... tshul dang po gsum gyi don nyung ngu'i ngag gis ston par byed pa'i legs par bshad pa tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa rin po che'i rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa'i don nyung ngu'i ngag gis gtan la 'bebs pa'i bstan bcos ljon shing mdzes pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... rnam thar dkar chag bzhugs so / /

dngul chu bla ma chos bzang ni /
rab byung bcu gsum pa'i chu pho 'brug gi lo zla ba dgu pa'i tshes dgu nyin par gtsang g.yas ru'i cha rong stod khyug mo'i yul du yab bkra shis dpal 'byor dang /
yum mkha' 'gro dpal skyid gnyis kyi sras su 'khrungs /
yul der yi ge shes mkhan dkon pa dang /
khyim gyi 'tsho bar dka' ba'i dbang gis /
dgung lo bcu gcig pa'i thog da gzod sku zhang rgan po lha bu zhes pa gcig yod pa de'i mdun nas ka kha sbyong ba'i dbu btsugs /
de nas mu mthud de yi ge shes mkhan su dang thug kyang cung zad re sbyong zhing /
ra lug rdzi bo byed zhor rdo leb ngos 'jam dang /
sa gzhi ngos snyoms sogs la mdzub mos yi ge bris nas /
mdzub rtse thengs mang rdol yang ci mi snyam par rgyun 'khyongs mdzad de yun mi ring bar /
dbu chen dbu chung tshang ma 'bri shes par gyur /
khyim na jo jo rta mgrin dbang rgyal min pa de min spun rnams lo na phra bas /
khong ni yab yum gyi sri zhu dang ra lug 'tsho ba sogs go chod pa zhig yod pas /
yun ring por khyim du gnas dgos byung /
'on kyang yi ge 'bri klog la thogs pa med par gyur /
khong dgung lo bcu gsum bzhes pa na /
bkra shis dge 'phel gyi grwa btsun mang pos /
yab yum la khong grwa pa byed dgos par bskul bar brten dgung lo bcu bzhi pa shing mo sbrul gyi lo'i zla ba dang por /
yab dang lhan cig tu bkra shis dge 'phel la phebs /
slob dpon blo bzang rgyal mtshan la skra phud phul te grwa pa byas /
ming blo bzang tshe ring btags /
nyin der gos ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan legs par bzhes nas gung tshogs su phebs /
khong gi dge rgan sku yon mi che yang /
tshul  khrims gtsang ba dang /
thugs rgyud drang la phan sems ldan pa zhig yin /
de nas khyim mtshes dbu mdzad shes rab mdun du cho ga'i skor rnams legs par gsan /
dgung lo bcu gsum pa'i lo de'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga'i phyi dror mkhas chen ngag dbang rdo rje'i drung du dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa rim can du blangs /
bsrung bya mtha' dag tshul bzhin bsrungs /
dgung lo bcu drug pa me lug lo'i ston khar dge rgan gyis khong la ja bag phyed /
mar nyag do /
rtsam pa bre bco lnga /
tshwa bul phran bu /
rdzas chas sne gsum /
gdan chung gcig bcas gnang nas sger du sdod bcug skabs der sku chas shin tu zhan mod /
tshogs pa na 'gyed chung re rnyed na'ang dpe cha blu ba sogs mdzad nas rang gi 'tsho ba ha cang ngan ngon kho nar bsten /
dgung lo bco brgyad par gcen po rta mgrin dbang rgyal dgung lo nyi shu'i thog sku gshegs par brten /
rang khyim du yab yum la sems gso'i ched du phebs te bsngo smon sogs 'don /
dgung lo bcu dgu pa lcags khyi lo'i zla ba dang por /
drin can gyi ma dgung grangs zhe gnyis las ma lon pa de dang /
brtse ldan gyi sru mo gnyis rgyu rims kyis dus gcig la 'das /
rang rang gi bza' btung tsam yang mi nus pa'i phru gu mang pos bskor ba'i pha rgad po gcig pur lus /
khong yid skyo ba tshad med bskyed de da ni sa dben pa zhig tu sgrub pa nyams len byed 'gro dgongs nas gnas tshul bla mar zhus /
bla mas dngul chu ri khrod du sdod rgyu byas na nye 'gyangs 'tsham zhing byin rlabs che bas der sdod ces gsungs /
dgung lo nyi shu pa lcags phag lor dngul chu ri khrod du phebs /
lo de'i zla ba bcu par slob dpon ye shes dpal grub drung nas dge slong gi sdom pa mnos /
dgung lo nyer gcig par blo bzang bskal bzang chos rgyal slob dpon du bsten nas gsan sbyong mdzad /
bla ma'i gsung rtsom 'ga'i phyag bris kyang khong gis mdzad /
'on kyang slob dpon lo gnyis tsam las ma bzhugs par sku gshegs /
dge rdzogs sogs kyang khong gis bsgrubs /
dgung lo nyer gnyis nas so gnyis bar lo bcu'i ring bkra shis lhun por thengs mang phebs te 'brong rtse blo bzang tshul khrims /
gu ge yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin /
grub dbang bskal bzang chos rgyal sogs slob dpon mkhas chen mang po la chos bka' mtha' yas pa zhus /
khyad par rje drung blo bzang dge 'dun drung du sgra dang snyan ngag sum rtags /
mngon brjod /
sdeb sbyor sogs gsan /
mdor na rig gnas che phra kun la mkhas pa chen por gyur te mkhas grub kyi grags pa kun tu khyab bo /
dgung lo so gcig bzhes pa'i lo de'i zla ba dgu par yab 'das /
dgung lo so gnyis par rtsa ba'i slob dpon mkhas grub chen po ngag dbang rdo rje sku gshegs /
dgung lo so lnga pa nas sgrub pa nyams len gtso bor mdzad /
khyad par zhe gcig pa nas rang g.yog rang gis byas te chu len pa'ang dge slong kha cig la bcol te /
nye gnyen sogs sku 'khor tshang ma  gdan sar brdzangs /
de nas bzung dgung lo brgyad cu'i bar gru 'dzin du 'chad nyan mdzad par thengs 'ga' phebs pa ma gtogs dus phal che ba dngul chu ri khrod du sgrub pa kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad /
dgung lo brgyad cur phebs pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i lcags mo phag gi lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad pa'i phyi dror dngul chu ri khrod du sku gshegs so /
khong gi gdan sa la bkra shis dge 'phel gling btags pa'i rgyu mtshan ni dgon 'di thog mar 'debs pa po stod 'brug bka' brgyud pa'i grub thob kun 'phel zhes pa de yin la /
bla ma des dgon der rang gi mtshan zur nas dras te bkra shis dge 'phel zhes btags /
rje nas dge lugs bla ma mgon po dpal zhes pas zhal ngo nam mkha' dbang rgyal gyis rgyab skyor byas par brten nas dge lugs su bsgyur /
'on kyang dgon pa'i ming ma 'gyur bar rang 'jags su gnas pa red /
slob ma mkhas chen ngag dbang snyan grags dang /
ri sbug sprul sku blo gsal bstan skyong /
bde chen sprul sku blo bzang tshul khrims sogs mang ngo /
khong gi gsung ni nged dpe mdzod khang du ka pa nas cha pa'i bar po ti drug bzhugs yod cing /
nang don rig pa'i skor dang khyad par gsang sngags kyi skor mang shos yin mod /
khong ni rig gnas kun la mkhas pa zhig yin pas /
deb ca pa'i nang <mkhas mchog si tu'i zhal lung> sogs sum rtags skor dang /
mngon brjod <rgya mtsho'i chu thigs> sogs dang /

... rje btsun ma yid bzhin 'khor lo la brten pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg mdor bsdus bya tshul zag med bdud rtsi'i gru char zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gzungs sngags mkho che ba 'ga' zhig klog 'don bya tshul bshad pa legs sbyar smra ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  khri gung thang pa chen pos mdzad pa'i sdom tshig gi sgo nas sdom pa gsum gyi mi mthun phyogs dran tshul bshad pa rab gsal nyin byed snang ba thub bstan padmo'i mdzes rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bslab bya mthong ba don ldan gyi tshig 'grel gnad don kun gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mchod rten gyi thig rtsa bklags pas 'grub pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon dkar gyi bum thod 'khor lo sgrub tshul 'dod rgu'i char 'bebs yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... nor gyi dbang phyug 'phags pa dzam+b+hala ser po gtso rkyang dang gzugs las byung ba'i nor rgyun ma ser mo'i bum bsgrub so sor bya tshul 'dod rgu'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  par ma /
... ga nye brgyud tshe khrid 'chi med rdo rje'i srog shing gi tshe dbang bskur tshul gsal bar bshad pa gnas gsum mkha' 'gro'i zhal lung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... khye'u rin chen zla bas zhus pa'i mdo don nyams su len tshul don gnyis lhun 'grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i bsnyen yig mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
...  dpal ldan lha mo la brten nas sho mo 'debs tshul nor bu'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'jig rten pa'i lha rten gyi nang du 'jug rgyu'i bum pa bsgrub tshul bde skyid nyi ma 'dren pa'i shing rta zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... brda sprod pa dbyangs can gyi mdo 'jam dbyangs bla mas 'gyur bcos mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... sum cu pa'i rtsa ba legs bshad ljon dbang /
... sum cu pa'i snying po'i don gsal byed legs bshad ljon pa'i dbang po bzhugs so / /
... rtags kyi 'jug pa'i snying po'i don mdo tsam brjod pa dka' gnad gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bod yig gi gnas dang byed rtsol ngos 'dzin tshul gsar pa'i gtam gyi myu gu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  ming gcig don mang po la 'jug tshul bshad pa blo gsal mgrin rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gsung thor bu phyogs bsgrigs bzhugs so / /
... rje bod mkhas pa'i gab tshig dper brjod logs su bkol te bshad pa mkhas dbang dgongs rgyan pan chen bla ma'i zhal lung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa dbyangs can grub pa'i rdo rje dpal bzang po'i gsung thor bu rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa bzhugs so / /
... skyabs mgon paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma'i mtshan sngags byings nas bsgrubs pa bzhugs so / /
... zab lam gcod kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs myur 'jug ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grwa tshang phyi mo'i chos bdag rgyal po chen por gsol mchod mdor bsdus bya tshul dgra lha dgyes pa'i rnga dbyangs bzhugs so / /
...  zhu 'phrin gyi rim pa kha shas bzhugs so / /
... dge slong blo bzang chos 'phel gyi dbyangs chung 'ga' zhig bzhugs / /
... zam par rab gnas bya tshul 'gyur med rdo rje'i lhun po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshogs mchod brgya tshar sogs 'bul tshul mdor bsdus mkha' 'gro dgyes byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  gangs can bstan 'gro'i mgon po paN chen mchog gi sprul pa'i sku'i mtshan sngags byings bsgrub byas pa legs bshad rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... zhwa ser bstan pa'i gsal byed hor khang gsar sprul pa'i sku nas bka' 'dri gnang pa'i lan bris pa'i mar me zhes bya ba sogs bzhugs / /
... rdo rje khyung lung ma zhi drag dang /
rgyal po li byin ha ra gnyis la mchod gtor gser skyems mdor bsdus stabs gcig tu 'bul tshul sogs bzhugs so / /
... sad srung ril bu bsgrub tshul bzhugs / /
... blo bzang 'jigs med dbang po'i mtshan bstod /
mtshan sngags /
yun brtan tshigs bcad bcas bzhugs / /
... brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs bzhugs so / /
... dam pa 'ga' zhig gi brtan bzhugs bzhugs so / /
... rdo rje phur pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi thig rtsa gsar ba'i legs bshad bzhugs so / /
... 'od dpag med kyi 'pho ba bka' rgya ma'i bka' zin bzhugs so / /
...  klu gtor mdor bsdus gtong tshul bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... byang chub ltung bshags dang spyi bshags gnyis kyi zin bris thar 'dod snying gi dga' ston zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dga' ldan rtsis gsar las nyi zlar sgra gcan 'jug tshul gzur gnas mkhas pa dgyes pa'i mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  rgya nag sa glang brtag tshul legs bshad yongs 'du'i shing dbang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsis kyi 'khor lo'i gsal byed bzhugs so / /
... ngo mtshar re'u mig las zhi gza' gnyis kyi rkang 'dzin bzhugs so / /
... ngo mtshar re'u mig las zhi gza' gnyis kyi dal dag bzhugs / /
...  ngo mtshar re'u mig las bkra shis nyin zhag la spyod pa'i dal dag bzhugs / /
... ngo mtshar re'u mig las bla ma nyin zhag la spyod pa'i dal dag bzhugs / /
... ngo mtshar re'u mig las nyi bu nyin zhag la spyod pa'i dal dag bzhugs / /
... ngo mtshar re'u mig las gza' lnga'i myur rkang bzhugs / /
...  rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /

dbyangs can grub pa'i rdo rje'am /
blo bzang chos 'phel gyi 'khrungs yul ni dbus gtsang khams gsum las gtsang g.yas ru'i bye brag bkra shis dge 'phel gling gi nye 'dabs /
sngon dus 'jad ces grags kyang /
rjes su slob dpon padmas yul de'i che ba'i dge mtshan la zhal 'dzum lan gsum grol bas bzhad ces pa'i ming thob pa der yin la /
yab d+harma b+ha dra'i gcung bkra shis dang yum tshe ring sri chod gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa mo sbrul lo zla ba bcu pa'i  tshes pa lnga'i dgong mor sku bltams /
dgung lo lnga par khu bo d+harma b+ha dra'i drung du ka kha sbyong ba'i 'go btsugs /
de dus byis pa'i ming 'jam dbyangs rdo rje zer /
lo grangs drug tsam ring bla ma'i mdun gsan sbyong byas pas sbyor sdeb blo 'dzin sogs la thogs pa med par gyur /
dgung lo bcu par bla ma'i gzim phug gi nye 'gram rgya ma brag phug ces par thob rgyal bla ma ngag dbang snyan grags mdun gsan sbyong mdzad par phebs /
zas gos sogs kyi mthun rkyen tshang ma khu bo bla ma nas sbyar /
rtsis kyi sa ris dang snyan ngag bcas la mkho ba'i mngon brjod sna tshogs blor 'dzin mdzad /
skabs der yum gyi ma ha cang gces pa'i rmol rmol zhig yod pa 'das nas /
rang khyim du skor tsam phebs /
de 'phral tshur log ste gsan sbyong la 'bad /
dgung lo bcu gcig par bkra shis dge 'phel dgon nas grwa khral sdud par brten /
khong yang grwa khral khongs nas grwa btsun mdzad /
dka' chen dkon mchog chos 'phel mdun du skra phud phul /
ming blo bzang chos 'phel btags /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par dka' chen dkon mchog chos 'phel drung nas dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos /
de nas bzung rje mi la'i rnam mgur dang ro sgrung sogs dang thig tshad dang blos bslangs bcas mthar phyin par sbyangs /
dgung lo bcu bdun par yab tshong la phebs pa jag pas bcom nas bkrongs /
ma dang nu mo bcas rjes su lus khong ma smad skyo ngal tshad med kyis mnar /
dgung lo nyi shur phebs pa na /
shar 'brog na mo che nas byang sta sgo'i bar gyi 'brog sde rnams su dbyar khar dgon pa'i dkar sdud la song nas zla ba gsum tsam 'gor /
de nas dgon pa'i tshogs shing gnyer pa lo 'gar mdzad /
mdor na dgon par dgung lo bcu gcig nas bcu dgu'i bar lo brgyad ring 'don rta dbyangs rol mo sogs nas blo 'dzin dgos rigs tshang ma legs par grub cing /
dbang lung sogs kyang mang po thob bo /
dgung lo bcu dgu pa nas bzung bla ma d+harma b+ha dra'i zhabs zhu pa mdzad de sgra dang rtsis /
snyan ngag dang sum rtags /
mdo dang sngags kyi gzhung chen mo rnams sbyong ba'i dbu tshugs /
dgung lo so bzhi par bla ma'i mdun snyan ngag dang sgra ka la pa'i rgyuD phul bas bla mas thugs dgyes pa chen pos leD so dang bcas lha rdzas srid du ring ba mgul par bstsal te /
mtshan dbyangs can grub pa'i rdo rje zhes pa gnang /
de nas bzung mtshan de kun bshad ming du gyur /
lo de'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga nyin bla ma chos bzang d+harma b+ha dra drung nas dge slong gi sdom pa mnos /
de nas bzung dge slong gi bslab bya'i 'khrid sogs 'dul ba'i skor gyi zab khrid rgya mtsho lta bu gsan /
bla ma'i thugs la zab chos bzhugs dgu bum pa gang byo'i tshul gyis zhu zhing rig gnas che phra kun la mkhas pa'i yang rtser son /
bla ma'i gsung rtsom 'ga'i yi ge pa'ang khong gis mdzad /
dgung lo zhe gsum du phebs pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i lcags mo phag gi lo'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes  brgyad nyin bla ma dam pa dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim /
lo nyer bzhi tsam bla ma dang 'bral med du gshibs pa'i dbang gis thugs skyo ba tshad med ngang nas /
pur khang brtsegs pa dang /
dngul gyi gdung rten bzhengs pa sogs dgongs rdzogs kyi bya ba tshang ma legs par bsgrubs /
bla ma'i rjes 'dzin mdzad de /
gdan sa rgya bskyed dang sku gsung thugs rten gsar bzhengs mdzad par ma tshad /
bla ma'i gsung 'bum rnams par brkos dang ljags zhu sogs kyang legs par mdzad /
dgung lo re gcig par sa skya dang bkras lhun brgyud dbus lha ldan du phebs /
dbus kyi dgon gnas dang rten khyad 'phags rnams la phyag mchod dang /
gdan sa gsum gyi bla chen rnams dang /
bka' blon bshad sgra sogs dpon chen rnams la dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi phul /
lo gcig lhag tsam 'gor rjes dgung lo re gnyis par gdan sar log bshad bsgrub gnyis kyi sgo nas dge ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan srid rtser bsgrengs /
gangs can mkhas pa yongs kyis gtsug gi tog ltar bkur /
khong dgung lo bdun cu don dgur phebs pa rab byung bco lnga pa'i me mo phag gi lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu drug la dgongs pa rdzogs so /
slob ma grags chen ngag dbang tshul khrims dang /
sgo mang lha rams pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho /
bla ma ye shes chos 'phel /
smin grol no mon han /
chab mdo 'phags pa lha /
chu bzang hu thog thu'u /
blo bzang 'jigs med sogs shin tu mang ngo /
khong gi gsung rab kyi rnam grangs ni bdun cu don grangs yod pa po ti ka nas ga'i bar gsum du bsdus pa cha tshang nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs shing /
nang don gsang sngags kyi skor mang tsam yod pa ma tshad /
snyan ngag skor <mkhas dbang dgongs rgyan> sogs dang <blo gsal mgron rgyan> sogs mngon brjod /
<rtsis kyi 'khor lo'i gsal byed> sogs rtsis kyi skor /
<thig rtsa gsar pa'i legs bshad> sogs thig tshad skor bcas ma tshad /
sum rtags skor <legs bshad ljon dbang> dang <dka' gnad gsal ba'i me long> ni kun gyis rgyus yod cing /
bod yig sbyong mkhan mang che bas blor 'dzin byed cing /
sum rtags mkhan po tshang mas tshad mar bzung ba red /
mdor na thun mong rig gnas skor la mdzad rjes lhag par che zhing khong gi rig gnas kyi gsung rab rnams ni kun gyis tshad mar 'dzin 'os pa sha stag yin no /

rnga rgod nam mkha' seng ge'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka 'dren mchog dam pa chos kyi rje nam mkha' seng ge dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa dpag bsam ljon pa dge legs 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grub dbang gur sdi rin po ches mdzad pa'i slob dpon nam mkha' seng ge'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs dang rgyal bstan ma gnyis bzhugs / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'khyer bde bzhugs / /
... byang chub bde lam gyi sbyor chos sogs bla ma'i zhal shes skal ldan 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bde lam gyi khrid dmigs skyong tshul 'don bsgrig tu bkod pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po'i bla brgyud smon lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur 'jug smon tshig bslu med mchog gsum ma sogs bzhugs / /
...  klu dbang rgyal po sgrub thabs bum chog byabs khrus dang bcas pa bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun byams mgon gyi sems bskyed sogs kyi rtogs brjod mdo sde las byung ba bzhugs so / /
...  kun rig gi bsnyen pa'i kha skong gi sbyin sreg gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... dus dgra'i dbang po'i sa chog sogs kyi lag len gyi rnam bshad gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'jigs byed kyi drag po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga lag tu blang bde ba bzhugs / /
... thig 'grel smin grol 'jug sgo gsal sgron zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi brgyud 'debs sman rag gtor gsum byin rlabs smon lam sogs bzhugs so / /
... rta mchog rol ba mnyes thabs sbyin sreg dngos grub kun stsol bzhugs so / /
... bcu cha'i sbyin sreg la blugs su tshogs pa shin tu nyung bsdus skal ldan re skong bzhugs so / /
... tshe bdag mgon po mkha' 'gro bzhis bskor yum bcas kyi sgrub thabs 'dod 'jo'i bum bzang bzhugs so / /
... ye shes kyi mgon po rgyan can gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs rim dang bcas pa skal ldan tshe gcig nyid la mkha' spyod rang zhal blta ba'i lam bzang zhes bya ba gu hya sa ma ya / /
... mgon po snying bzhugs kyi mngon rtogs bzhugs so / /
... ma hA kA la'i tshogs 'khor bsdus pa bzhugs so / /
...  rab gnas kyi cho ga phan bde'i ku mud bzhad pa'i zla shel zhes bya ba bi ha ra tisma / /
... mgon po'i thun las dang drug cu pa rgyas bsdus gnyis bzhugs / /
... mgon po phyag drug pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dngos grub char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po phyag drug pa'i las bzhi'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga mdor bsdus 'dod don lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dul ba'i bslab bya nyung bsdus blo gsal dga' ston zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dul ba'i bslab bya nyung gsal ltung mun gdung sel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sdom pa gong ma gnyis kyi bslab bya'i sdom tshig gi mchan 'grel nyes ltung mun sel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'tsho ba'i yo byad ji ltar 'chang tshul byin gyis rlabs tshul sogs bzhugs so / /
... thar pa chen po'i mtshan phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa bzhugs so / /
... snod bcud kyi rnam gzhag ngo mtshar kun gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... kha gsung 'bum gyi dkar chag mthong don rab gsal mal+li ka'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  gsol 'debs bshad bsgrub bstan 'phel ma bzhugs so / /
... smyung bar gnas pa'i cho ga nag 'gros su bkod pa bde chen gsal ba bzhugs / /
... smyung gnas kyi cho ga bsdus pa bzhugs / /
... 'jam dbyangs nA ga rak+Sha'i sgrub thabs bum sgrub dang bcas pa bzhugs / /
... mchog pur la brten mchod yul mnyes byed mchod sprin dngos grub char 'bebs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mchod rten gyi rnam bzhag phan bde'i gsos gyur ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rten bshad grangs med dge legs ma rten tho kun gsal me long bkra shis bshad sgrub gling gi jo bo'i sku brnyan mthong ba don ldan gyi rten bshad rnams bzhugs so / /
... srid pa'i 'khor lo cha lnga pa'i 'bri tshul bzhugs so / /
...  mchod khang gsar bskrun gyi dkar chag gsal ba'i me long bzhugs so / /
... mchod khang gsar bskrun gyi logs bris mchod rten zhal byang phan bde kun stsol zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bca' yig blang dor gsal byed bzhugs so / /
... dkon brtsegs kyi bris byang bsngo smon tshar gnyis dang bsngo ba bcas bzhugs so / /
...  byA ka ra Na sum cu pa dang rtags kyi 'jug pa gnyis bzhugs so / /
... sum rtags kyi 'grel ba nyung gsal blo ldan dga' bskyed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... snyan dngag gi legs bshad kun mkhyen lnga pa'i zhal lung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... skar rtsis kyi sngon 'gro sogs nyer mkho bzhugs so / /
...  lnga bsdus sogs kyi rtsis gzhi gsar spos bai dkar las 'phros bdud rtsi'i zegs ma bzhugs so / /
... lnga bsdus gza' lnga sogs kyi rtsis gzhi gsar spos bai dkar las 'phros bdud rtsi'i zegs ma sogs sa ri'i skor rnams bzhugs so / /
... byed grub rtags longs 'dod lnga dbugs sgang khyim 'pho ri phag nyi ldog bcas kyi re'u mig bzhugs so / /
... grub mtha'i rtsis kyi bskal li skar drug chu tshod zhe lngas sbyangs pa bzhugs so / /
... grub mtha'i rtsis kyi cha shas re'u mig stong 'og 'khor ma bzhugs so / /
... gza' lnga nyin tshes rtags longs rkang nor gyi re'u mig bzhugs so / /
... las rtsis zur bkol nyung gsal phan bde'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... keg rtsis kyi lde mig sogs de'i skor 'ga' bzhugs so / /
...   thang shing ring mo'i rtsis las legs par btus pa bzhugs so / /
... bai dkar bag rtsis las lo 'gres sdeb tshul sogs ri'u mig tu bsgrigs shing nyung ngur bsdus pa gsal byed me long zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... man ngag lhan thabs ltar gyi nad rtags ngos 'dzin gsal bar ston byed ha nu ma n+tha'i rol rtsed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  gter gsar gur drag gi las tshogs las 'phros tshe sgrub kyi cho ga 'chi med rdo rje'i lhun po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /

rnga rgod nam mkha' seng ge ni /
mdo smad rngog phyogs kyi sa yi char gtogs pa gser bo zhes pa'i yul du /
yab mgon po tshe ring dang /
yum ban de mtsho gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i chu pho 'brug gi lo la 'khrungs /
dgung grangs lnga pa'i dus su /
ngar rgod dpon gyis bkas bskul 'og chos 'khor zhabs drung rin po che nas /
rnga rgod bla ma dka' bcu rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi sprul skur ngos bzung /
dgung lo bdun par 'bo ra nas phebs pa'i btsun pa zhig dge rgan du bsten nas klog slob pa'i dbu btsugs /
'dul 'dzin chen po tA dpon sprul sku'i mdun du rab tu byung zhing dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
mtshan nam mkha' seng ge zhes gsol /
lo de'i zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin par mdzad sgo'i rten 'brel gzab rgyas dang bcas bla ma gong ma'i gdan khrir bzhugs /
khu bo rab 'byams smra ba blo bzang dpal 'byor yongs 'dzin du bsten nas /
rje mi la'i rnam mgur gyi khrid lung dang /
kun rig dang 'jigs byed sogs kyi dbang rjes gnang bcas mang du zhus par ma zad /
dam pa de nyid la sman gyi rgyud bzhi'i lag len sogs gsan cing /
rgyud kyi rtsa ba blor 'dzin mdzad /
rtse dbus pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan mdun du /
dbyangs can sgra mdo'i ri mo sogs sgra'i skor dang /
rtsis skar nag dang thig tshad sogs tha snyad rig pa'i gnas rnams la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad /
dgung lo bcu dgu par  'dul 'dzin chen po tA dpon pas mkhan po mdzad nas dge slong gi sdom pa gnang /
lo der dbus gtsang du gnas skor phebs /
dbon rgan gzhon gnyis dang khu tshan bcas bzhi po lhan cig tu dbus gdan sa gsum dang /
gtsang bkra shis lhun po sogs dgon gnas khag dang /
der bzhugs kyi rten khyad 'phags rnams mjal bar ma tshad /
tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho mgar thar nas dbus su byon ma thag pa'ang mjal kha thob /
bkras lhun du paN chen rin po che'ang mjal nas /
gra sar ma zhugs par khu bo dang dbon rgan gyis gsung dang bstun te ring min rang gi gdan sar log dgung lo nyer lnga pa me 'brug lor khu bo yongs 'dzin blo bzang dpal 'byor dgongs pa rdzogs /
chung dus nas 'dris che ba'i dbang gis thugs skyo gdung tshad med ngang nas /
dgongs rdzogs kyi bya ba rgya chen bsgrubs /
dgung lo so gcig par gyi ling ri khrod du phebs nas sgrub pa nyams len mdzad cing rjes nas gzim mnal brtags pa'i ltas sogs la brten /
shing bzo sangs rgyas skyabs la gsas mkhar sgang du shing gi mtshams khang zhig 'debs bcug ste mtshams bzhugs /
lo shas rjes 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa 'jigs med dbang po mjal bar phebs /
'jam bzhad nas a mchog gi sar dgon pa zhig 'debs na /
phyis 'phel rgyas rgya che yong rgyu sogs kyi bka' nan gnang bar brten /
khong gis a mchog gi yul du dgon pa gsar du btab /
rjes nas bshad gra dang sgrub gra btsugs /
sku gsung thugs kyi rten mang po gsar bzhengs dang /
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi chos sprin rgya cher spros /
mdo smad kyi stag tshang dgon dang /
khya dge dgon /
dgon lung /
rkang tsha dgon sogs dgon gnas phal che bar phebs shing bla sprul dang dpon khag rnams la dam pa'i chos char phab cing /
dben par sgrub pa nyams len mdzad mkhan rnams la'ang gang la gang 'tsham gyi bka' chos gnang nas /
dgung lo re dgu ru phebs pa rab byung bcu gsum pa'i lcags pho byi ba'i lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes gcig nyin pa'i tho rangs kyi dus su dgongs pa zhi ba'i dbyings su thim mo /
khong gi gsung rab kyi rnam grangs ni <bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'khyer bde> dang <byang chub bde lam gyi sbyor chos> sogs mdo sngags kyi nyams len dang khrid chog sogs bdun cu lhag tsam dang /
<sum rtags 'grel pa blo ldan dga' bskyed> dang <snyan ngag gi legs bshad kun mkhyen lnga pa'i zhal lung> dang <skar rtsis sngon 'gro> sogs rig gnas thun mong ba'i gsung rab bcu lhag bcas khyon gsung rab brgyad cu tsam bzhugs pa gcig tu bsdus te po ti ka pa dang kha pa gnyis byas pa nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod /

rnga rgod blo bzang byams pa rab rgyas kyi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka mkhas grub chen po rnam gnyis kyi rnam thar dang rang gi spyod tshul gsal bar ston pa dwangs shel me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun bla ma mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug nges pa don gyi kun spangs chen po ngag dbang stobs ldan pa'i rnam thar mdo tsam brjod pa dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... blo sbyong thar pa'i them skas blo gsal 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po 'od dpag med la bsten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor bde ba can gyi myur lam zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa tshe'i bdag po'i tshe 'gugs mi shigs srog gi chad mthud ces bya ba bzhugs / /
... dpal 'khor lo bde mchog dkar po'i sbyin sreg 'bul tshul dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dzaM b+ha la dkar po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga dngos grub sgo 'byed zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dzam dmar chags pa rdo rje'i 'jam po gsum gyi sbyin sreg dngos grub bang mdzed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor dzam dmar gyi chu sbyin dang chags pa rdo rje'i bskangs bshags bzhugs so / /
... rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi g.yang 'gugs don yod 'phrul 'khor zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bde 'dus kyi sgo nas tshe ldan la sbyang chog byed tshul dag byed bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong can gyi rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma bdud 'dul seng ge'i gdong ba can gyi sgo nas sri mnan byed tshul rdo rje lhun po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong ba can gyi sgo nas byad 'grol byed tshul bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma bdud 'dul drag mo'i sbyin sreg bya tshul 'dod don kun 'grub bzhugs so / /
... grub dbang padma 'byung gnas la phul ba'i 'phrin yig thugs rje bskul ba'i gdung dbyangs bzhugs so / /
... dpal myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i bsnyen yig mdor bsdus bklag pas kun shes dngos grub bang mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  bla mgon dbyer med la brten pa'i rnal 'byor dang bsnyen pa byed tshul mdor bsdus phan bde'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug par phyi rten 'bul tshul dngos grub gru char g.yo ba'i sprin phung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gzi brjid rgyal mo'i mdos chog gdung sel zla zer zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yul lha'i bsangs mchod kyi skor bzhugs so / /
... klu rgyal chab brag sogs kyi bsangs mchod bzhugs so / /
... lha gnyan chen po sngon lha g.yu rtse'i bsangs mchod 'dod don kun 'grub zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ma cig dpal lha'i gtor chog bsam 'phel nor bu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sku gsung thugs rten gsar bzhengs kyi dkar chags mgo rgyan dang smon tshig skor bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... kha gru 'dzin zhing gi smon lam rin chen them skas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... brgya rtsa gnad don kun tshang bzhugs so / /
... 'jam dpal nag po'i bum chog 'khyer bde dngos grub kun stsol zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  mchog khrus byed tshul dag byed bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bsngo ba phan bde mchog sbyin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... chos la bskul ba'i bslab bya thar ba'i sgo 'byed zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bslab bya lhag bsam 'od dkar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshangs sras lha mo'i sgrub thabs shes rab mchog sbyin bzhugs so / /
... zab lam gcod kyi nyams len byang sems myu gu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... zab lam gcod dang 'brel ba'i smon lam rgyal sras 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshogs mchod don gnyis lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i tshogs 'khor rgyun khyer 'dod rgu'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal po'i lugs kyi thugs rje chen po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga sdig mun sel ba'i zla gzhon bzhugs so / /
... thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i bsnyen yig bklags pas don 'grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gnas chen gyi rang bzhin brjod pa rgyud mangs sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  zhabs brtan gsol 'debs drang srong bden tshig ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe 'gugs rdo rje'i srog sbyin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  mgon po dzaM b+ha la dkar po'i gter dang chu sbyin sbrags tshul dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ma cig rdo rje g.yu sgron ma'i tshe g.yang 'gugs tshul don yod zhags pa'i 'phrul 'khor zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... nor bdag skyes bu chen po'i g.yang 'bod don zhags 'phrul 'khor zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po yid bzhin nor bu'i g.yang 'bod legs tshogs 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha sman mched gsum dang ye shes khye'u chung gi rjes gnang bklags pas don grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ri khrod dbang mo rnam gsum gyi sgrub thabs bum chog dang bcas pa gdung sel zla ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gsol 'debs legs tshogs sgo 'byed ces bya ba sogs bzhugs so / /
...  ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong ba can gyi bsnyen yig mdor bsdus bklags pas kun shes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...   mgon po tshogs kyi bdag po'i las byang dam can rol mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe dbang bya tshul 'khyer bde bzhugs so / /
... bslab bya snying gtam gros 'debs bzhugs so / /
... myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po la mchod gtor 'bul tshul dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gnas chen shel dkar gyi gnas kyi rang bzhin brjod pa khu byug mgrin pa'i rgyang glu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bde gsang 'jigs gsum gyi bsnyen yig nag 'gros su bkod pa bklags pas kun shes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dam can rdo rje legs pa ra zhon gyi gtor chog las bzhi lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das rgyal ba mi 'khrug pa'i sgo nas ser ba srung ba'i man ngag bzhugs so / /
... rlung rta'i kwa 'dzugs mi shigs srog sbyin bsod nams dpal bskyed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... snyan ngag le'u gsum gyi dper brjod dpyid kyi pho nya'i mgrin glu zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rig 'dzin gdung sgrub kyi rgyun 'khyer bklags pas don grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha mo nor rgyun ma'i g.yang 'bod don yod zhags pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  zhing skyong dbang po'i gtor 'bul gdug pa tshar gcod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dkar chag gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

rnga rgod blo bzang byams pa rab rgyas ni mdo smad kyi sa'i char shis tshang zhes pa'i yul du /
yab gzungs 'bum rgyal dang /
yum klu mo gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gsum pa'i lcags mo glang gi lo zla ba gnyis par sku bltams /
'khrungs ma thag tu /
khri chen blo bzang nyi mas dkon mchog skyabs zhes pa'i ming btags /
dgung grangs lnga par 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa 'jigs med dbang pos rnga rgod nam mkha' seng ge'i sku skye ru ngos bzung /
dgung lo drug par bkra shis 'khyil du tshogs chen khri pa rab brtan rgya mtsho'i drung du grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang zhus /
dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsir thog mar rol /
dgung lo bdun bzhes pa na /
khri chen blo bzang nyi ma'i drung du rab tu byung /
ming blo bzang bstan pa rab rgyas btags /
de nas klog slob pa'i mgo btsugs /
lo de'i zla ba bcu pa'i tshes gcig nyin par rang khyim nas btegs te /
nya 'ban rgyal ri thang sogs brgyud nas tshes lnga nyin par bla ma gong ma'i gdan sa bkra shis bshad sgrub gling du 'byor /
dge 'dun pa rnams kyis ser sgreng gzab rgyas dang bcas bsus te gdan khrir bkod /
dgung lo brgyad par /
dran dbang mkhas btsun seng ge'i zhabs drung du bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam sogs sbyor klog dag par bslabs /
btsun pa 'jam dbyangs shes rab slob dpon du bskos /
dgung lo dgu par shugs yag ri khrod du phebs /
ye shes rgya mtsho'i spyan sngar dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos /
'dul ba'i bslab bya rnams zhib khrid dang gung tshigs sogs ma chag par byas /
dgung lo bcu par lha 'brum btab /
rje gong ma'i dngos slob sman pa dge legs kyis co ne mkhan po'i mdun nas sman 'khyer yong ba bzhes pas myur du bde bar grol /
khong gi 'brum kog la brten nas byis pa brgya lhag 'brum nad las thar /
dgung lo bcu gcig par rang yul du phebs /
ser skya mang tshogs rnams la grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang bskur /
sgros dag cing gsal la lhag chad med pas /
pha khu sogs dga' spro chen po bskyed /
dgung lo bcu gnyis nas bco brgyad bar lo bdun ring /
dge ba'i bshes gnyen du mar bsten nas dbang lung khrid sogs zhus shing khong rang nyid nas kyang dbang lung sogs gnang /
dgung lo bcu dgu par drin che ba'i yum dus kyi chos nyid  du gyur par brten /
thugs skyo ba chen pos kun rig gi sbyangs chog nan tan bgyis shing /
bla brang dgon nas gung thang rin po che gdan drangs nas /
'pho ba dang sbyangs chog gshin dbang sogs kyi bka' drin bstsal /
lo der khri chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mkhan slob sbrags ma gnang nas /
dge 'dun grangs tshang dbus su bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa mnos /
slob dpon blo bzang rgyal mtshan dang /
dpal mang rin po che sogs la dbang lung khrid bcas mang du zhus /
dgung lo nyer dgu pa sa sbrul lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i nang /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa 'jigs med rgya mtsho dang lhan cig tu dbus gtsang du gnas skor phebs /
dbus dang gtsang gi dgon gnas yongs la mjal skor phebs te rten khyad 'phags rnams la mar me snyan shal dang /
ris med gra mang yongs la mang 'gyed phul /
tA la'i dgu ba sku na phra yang mjal ba'i dus su zhal 'dzum dang bcas khams 'dri sogs gsung gsal gnang /
bkra shis lhun por paN chen rin po che la chos 'brel zhus /
dbus gtsang la lo gcig tsam 'gor rjes /
rang lo sum cu pa lcags rta zla ba bdun par gdan sa bkra shis bshad sgrub gling du tshur phebs /
gtsug lag khang gsar btab dang /
lha sku gsar bzhengs /
gser dngul gyi gsung rab gsar bris sogs rnam dkar gyi 'phrin las rgya chen po spel /
dgung lo zhe gsum par khong la bya ba las kyi 'khor lo bskor bar lhag bsam rnam dag gis phan grogs mdzad po drin can gyi slob dpon de nyid /
rim gro sman bcos la 'bad kyang ma 'tsho bar lnga lam du gsheD pas thugs khral tshad med byung rung bya thabs bral zhing /
bkra shis 'khyil sogs dgon chen rnams su mang 'gyed dang /
bla chen rnams la bsngo rten phul ba sogs dgongs rdzogs kyi bya ba legs par bsgrubs /
dgung lo zhe brgyad par rnga khog phyogs kyi dgon gnas rnams su phebs te chos sbyin bstsal /
zhe dgu par sog yul gyi dgon khag rnams su phebs /
dgung lo re dgu ru phebs pa /
rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa mo bya'i lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes nyi shu nyin gyi snga dror dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim mo /
khong gi gsung ni sne grangs lnga bcu nga bzhi yod pa po ti ka pa dang kha pa gnyis su bsdus pa zhig nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod cing /
nang don phal mo che tshe 'gugs dang sbyin sreg bsnyen yig bsangs mchod sogs 'don cha'i cho ga'i skor yin pa dkar chag dang /
chab shog bslab bya'i skor bcas kyang 'ga' zhig yod do /

co ne grags pa bshad sgrub kyi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka slob dpon bshad sgrub ming can gyis brtsams pa'i dpe tho rin chen 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /
... mdo sngags chos brgyud kyi bla rabs bshad pa dngos grub 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /
... rgyud sde rnam bzhi'i dgongs 'grel sngags rim chen mo'i dgongs pa yang gsal sgron me legs par bshad pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yi dam sgrub skor 'dod dgu 'byung ba'i za ma tog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dus pa'i bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad gnad don kun gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim rim lnga gsal ba'i sgron me'i snying po bsdus pa skal ldan dgyes byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lU hi pa'i bskyed rim 'dod 'jo'i dgongs pa rab gsal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grub chen lU hi pa'i lugs kyi rdzogs rim rnal 'byor chen po'i rnam bshad dngos grub snye ma'i gnad don snying po gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rim pa dang po'i khrid rgyun man ngag snang brnyan kun 'char gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rim pa gnyis pa'i rnam bshad dngos grub snye ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grub chen dril bu'i zhabs lugs kyi bde mchog lha lnga'i bskyed rdzogs gnyis kyi 'khrid dmigs bde chen myur 'grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i rim gnyis snying po rin chen snye ma zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'dus pa'i rtsa rgyud dang bde mchog gi skor nas stong nyid bstan tshul gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... kha slob dpon bshad sgrub ming can gyis brtsams pa'i dpe tho rin chen 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /
... dmigs brtse ma'i tshig 'grel me tog phreng mdzes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga'i don mdor bsdus gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyud kyi rgyal po mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i snying po'i don 'grel gsal ba bzhugs so / /

...   bsnyen yig rin chen phreng mdzes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... lha lnga'i sgrub thabs bde chen yang gsal sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dril bu lha lnga'i bla brgyud smon lam shis brjod mdor bsdus pa / /
... 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i bla brgyud gsol 'debs smon lam shis brjod dang bcas pa mdor bsdus / /
... kun rig gi chog bsgrigs ngag 'don bya tshul 'jug ngogs bde ba'i lam zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ngan song sbyong ba'i thabs 'jug ngogs bde ba'i lam zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshe chog 'chi med dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... tshe ril bsgrub tshul 'chi med dpal sbyin / /

... dge slong ma dpal mo'i lugs kyi zhal bcu gcig pa'i sgrub thabs smyung bar gnas pa'i cho ga phan bde'i 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /
... mdo chog yid bzhin nor bu'i lhan thabs rin chen bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... dmigs brtse ma'i ril sgrub dang 'brel ba'i char 'bebs kyi las tshogs phan bde'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dkon mchog gsum dang skyabs 'gro'i rnam gzhag gsal bar bstan pa dngos grub 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... mdo nas dngos su gsungs pa'i bslab bya mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
...  skyes bu gsum dang bslab pa gsum dang thos bsam sgom gsum gyi dka' gnas legs par bshad pa'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rnam gzhag legs bshad snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mdo rgyud zab mo'i gnad don 'khor ba'i 'jug rim thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i khyad par bshad pa don gyi snying po gsal ba zhes bya bzhugs so / /
... gtor 'bul mdor bsdus / /
... par ma /
... ga slob dpon bshad sgrub ming can gyis brtsams pa'i dpe tho rin chen 'byung gnas bzhugs so / /

... lam rim sogs nas 'byung ba'i nyams len gyi rim pa dang yan lag bdun pa byed tshul rnam pa gnyis bzhugs so / /
... byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i 'khrid yig snying po'i don bsdus pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... sa lam gyi rnam gzhag mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  sdom pa gsum gyi rnam grangs bstan pa don bsdus gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bden bzhi dang rten 'brel gyi rnam par gzhag pa thar lam gsal byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dus tshigs kyi rnam gzhag legs par bshad pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dbu ma'i lugs kyi zab don gyi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grub mtha' thams cad kyi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... grub mtha' bzhi'i lugs kyi bden gnyis kyi rnam gzhag legs par bshad pa'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i snying po bdag med rtogs pa'i lta ba'i rim pa rnam par bshad pa thar lam gsal byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i don gyi snying po gsal byed kyi snang ba chen po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yum gyi mdo'i 'gres rkang gsal bar byed pa mkhas pa'i 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sems bskyed kyis rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob tshul brgal lan dogs gcod yum gyi mdo'i dgongs don cha shas kyi snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... skyabs 'gro'i dmigs rim thar pa'i sgo 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  lam gyi gtso bo rnam gsum gyi don 'grel gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bar do'i gsol 'debs kyi rnam bshad gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... sngags kyi bklag thabs smra ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gzhung lugs du ma'i brjod bya sna tshogs pa ming gi sgo nas gsal bar bstan pa nyer mkho blo ldan dga' byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mngal du 'jug pa'i mdo'i dgongs pa gsal bar byed pa'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... las kyi sgrib pa rgyun gcod pa'i mdo'i don nyams su len tshul bsod nams kyi 'byung gnas chen po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  tshogs gsog cing dkor sgrib sbyong byed gang+g+'I chu rgyun zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgya skad dang sngags don thor bu bod skad du bkrol ba bzhugs so / /

co ne grags pa bshad sgrub ni /
mdo smad co ne dpon po'i mnga' 'og tho'u ju'i yul gyi bye brag g.yo sa'am rab po zhes pa'i sa char /
yab gzungs skyabs 'bum dang /
yum bskal bzang sman gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gcig pa'i shing mo yos kyi lo zla ba dang po'i tshes brgyad la sku bltams /
'khrungs ma thag par yum tshad nad kyis mnar bas 'o ma ster ma nus /
khong gi jo mo rtswa mo mtshos thabs byas nas gsos /
dgung lo bdun par yab sogs kyi mdun nas 'bri klog slob pa'i dbu btsugs /
dgung lo dgu par khri chen dge 'dun grags pa'i spyan sngar rab tu byung /
de nas lo 'ga'i ring cho ga phyag len gyi skor blor 'dzin dgos rigs rnams sbyangs /
sman pa stag ris dge slong mdun du sman dpe 'ga' zhig sbyangs te /
nad par lag  rtsa lta ba sogs nad bcos kyi bya ba'ang cung zad bsgrubs /
dgung lo nyer gcig pa shing mo phag gi lo'i ston khar dbus lha ldan du phebs /
lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig par lha sar 'byor /
byi ba lo'i zla ba dang por ra mo cher se ra'i grwa tshang gi chos grwar zhugs /
der bkra shis dpal bzang dge rgan du bsten nas /
rgyan 'jug gnyis dang bsdus dpe thar thor blor 'dzin byed /
skabs de dag tu mtshan mor gnyid kyang spangs te 'bad par mdzad /
de nas rim gyis gzhung pod rnams la thos bsam byas nas dbus su lo bcur song ba shing mo bya'i lor /
slob dpon tshul khrims rin chen gyi bka' ltar /
smon lam chen mor grwa skor byas te ming rtags blang rtsis kyi skabs su /
dbus su dus 'khrug byung nas sde srid sku gshegs /
de'i dgongs rdzogs su zla ba brgyad par /
dbus kyi grub mtha' ris med kyi 'dun sde nyi khri lhag tsam tshogs /
skabs der gzhung nas smon lam chen mo ltar ming gdags dgos par bka' phebs /
bla mas khong la de ring mtshan rtags blang dgos gsungs par brten /
de bzhin bsgrubs pas /
ming btags legs par thob cing /
bla ma'ang shin tu thugs dgyes te legs so sbyin /
khong gdong gral du bzhugs su bcug dgung lo so gcig pa me pho khyi'i lor gtsang du phebs nas bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blangs /
de nas tshur log ste dga' ldan dang /
'bras spungs bcas su zhag 'ga' re bzhugs nas dam bca' bzhag pas /
tshang ma ngo mtshar ba byung zhing /
dam bca'i lan la thogs pa med par grags /
dgung lo so gnyis su phebs pa me mo phag gi lor /
dge slong blo gros rgya mtsho dang /
tshong pa dge 'dun dar rgyas sogs rang yul ba rnams kyis bskul bar brten /
lo de'i dpyid kar tshong pa dang 'grogs nas rang yul mdo smad du log zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco lngar mtsho sngon po'i khar 'byor /
der grong chog zla ba drug tsam song ba'i dkor yon des rta khal 'ga' nyos nas rang yul du yong /
zla ba bcu par drin can gyi yab yum lhan rgyas dang zhal 'dzoms thub pa byung bas smra mi shes pa'i dga' tshor byung /
skabs de dag tu co ne bstan pa'i mnga' bdag ko'i shrI nang so yes de nyid pho brang du gong ma rgyal po mjal ba'i tshe /
gong mas yes la khyod kyi dgon pa der mtshan nyid grwa tshang zhig tshugs zhes bka' phebs pa zhal gyis bzhes te /
shing rta lo'i zla ba bzhi par mtshan nyid grwa tshang btsugs /
grags pa bshad sgrub grwa tshang bla mar bskos /
khong dgung lo zhe gcig pa shing mo lug gi lor yum drin can dus kyi chos nyid du gyur /
thugs skyo ba chen po'i ngang nas dge rtsa btang /
lcags mo glang gi lor /
khong gis thugs rtsis shin tu che ba'i tsha bo bs+t+na 'dzin shes rab 'brum nad kyis shi bas thugs skyo ba tshad med byung ste grwa tshang slob dpon dgongs pa zhus /
rang gi gzim shag tu lo bdun tsam ring lam gyi gtso bo rnam gsum sogs dpe cha 'ga' brtsams te bzhugs /
me mo lug  gi lor /
nang so yes kyis slar khri la bzhugs dgos pa'i bka' nan phebs pa zlog tu ma btub par khas blangs /
sa mo bya'i lor rgyud pa grwa tshang btsugs te bla ma dang mkhan po zung 'brel mdzad /
de nas bzung dgung lo re gnyis bar 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis dus gron par mdzad de /
dgung grangs re gnyis su phebs pa na dgongs pa zhus pa 'khrol bas /
thugs shin tu dgyes te khri zur bzhugs /
legs bshad brtsams pa dang grong chog phebs pa bcas mdzad cing /
dgung lo bdun cu don bzhi lnga tsam la sku gshegs pa yin nam snyam /
khong gi gsung ni bon po'i skor gyi dpe cha 'ga' mchis 'dug kyang par du brkos yod med ma nges /
nang pa'i skor gsung 'bum du gzhugs yod pa'i rigs ni /
dbu ma dang /
phar tshad /
'dul ba bcas kyi gzhung 'grel dang /
mngon brjod /
dag yig snyan dngags /

lcang skya ngag dbang blo bzang chos ldan ni mdo smad tsong kha'i nyer 'dabs g.yi dge'i lung par rta phyug ces pa'i grong du /
yab khe ba cang e har dang /
yum lo za thar mo mtsho gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gcig pa'i chu pho rta'i lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu'i dgong mo mtshan phyed la sku bltams /
dgung grangs gsum bzhir phebs skabs da dung smra mi shes pa'i lkug pa lta bur gyur /
de nas yab yum gyis gtsang sbra sogs thabs sna tshogs la 'bad cing dge bsnyen bsgrub bcug pas rim gyis smra shes par gyur /
de gar bod pa bla rgan zhes pa'i bla ma zhig bzhugs pa des /
khong la dge 'dun skyabs zhes pa'i mtshan gsol /
de nas ring po ma lon par thang ring dgon gyi khri pa tshul khrims rgya mtshos yab la bu 'dir khrid shog ces dgon par bos /
bla ma gong ma grags pa 'od zer gyi dngos chas rnams ngos 'dzin byed bcug dbus lha ldan du bzhugs yod pa'i bla ma gong ma'i dbon po blo gros 'od zer mdun /
byis pa'i gnas tshul sogs kyi 'phrin yig phul /
blo gros 'od zer gyis paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan la gnas tshul snyan zhu phul bas /
paN chen nas grags pa 'od zer gyi sku skye ru ngos 'dzin mdzad de /
re zhig thang ring dgon du zhog ces pa'i bka' gnang /
de nas thang ring dgon du song nas /
dgon de'i khri zur tshul khrims rgya mtsho dang /
khri pa phun tshogs bzang po gnyis kyi spyan sngar gtsug phud phul te rab tu byung /
ming bstan 'dzin legs bshad rgya mtshor btags /
sbyor klog dang blor 'dzin gyi dbu tshugs /
dgung grangs dgu par dgon lung dga' ldan byams pa gling du phebs /
mchod yon kun gyis brtsi 'jog chen po byas /
dgung lo bcu gcig par /
tsong kha'i stod skar ma'i thang chen du /
lnga pa chen po pe cing du phebs pa mjal bar phyin /
dgung lo nyi shur phebs pa lcags mo glang gi lor dbus lha ldan du phebs /
lnga pa chen po mjal zhing khong gi spyan sngar dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos /
blo bzang chos ldan zhes pa'i ming gnang /
de nas dgon khag dang gnas khyad 'phags rnams su mjal skor zin rjes /
'bras spungs sgo mang grwa tshang gi chos grwar zhugs /
sgo mang slob dpon ngag dbang blo gros rgya mtsho'i spyan sngar lo brgyad ring tshad ma sogs gsan /
dgung lo nyer gsum pa shing pho 'brug gi lor /
rgyal dbang lnga pa'i mdun bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blangs /
dgung lo nyer bdun par gling bsre'i grwa skor dang /
nyer dgu par lha sa smon lam chen mor grwa skor mdzad /
dgung lo so gsum par /
gtsang du phebs /
paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan gyi sku phreng mjal /
shar rtse'i mkhan mo blo bzang padma la tsong kha pa dang /
paN chen gong ma'i gsung 'bum gyi khrid lung bcas zhus /
de rjes su'ang gtsang du thengs 'ga' phebs cing /
paN chen gong ma'i thugs sras dkon mchog rgyal mtshan sogs mkhas pa mang po slob dpon du bsten nas mdo sngags kyi gzhung rnams la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad de mkhas pa chen por gyur /
dgung lo zhe gnyis pa chu mo phag gi lor /
dgon lung dgon gyis bsu ma mngags pa dang lhan cig tu /
mdo smad du tshur phebs /
dgon lung ri khrod byang chub gling du bzhugs /
phyi lor thang ring dgon dang sku 'bum sogs su phebs /
dgung lo zhe drug par /
lo gsar smon lam chen po 'tshogs pa dang /
gong ma mjal ba'i ched du /
pe cing la khri chen ngag dbang blo gros rgya mtsho mnyam por lan gnyis byon /
lan dang por gong mas gos dar sogs kyi gnang sbyin bstsal cing zhal 'dri gnang /
lan gnyis par gong ma chen por dam pa'i chos kyi 'bel gtam phul /
gong mas thugs dgyes pa chen po mdzad cing mgul dar dang /
pe cing sdod dgos pa'i bka' lung bstsal /
gnas skabs pe cing bsdad mi dgos pa'i dgongs pa nan tan gyis zhus nas khrol /
dgung lo nga gnyis pa chu mo bya'i lor gong mas drung du yong dgos pa'i bka' lung lci ba phab /
gyen bzlog ma nus par rim gyis lam du zhugs /
pe cing pho brang gi nye skor du slebs pa na /
pho brang nang gi bla ma kun bsu bar phebs /
phyi lo'i ston khar rje btsun dam pa pe cing du phebs /
khong dang lhan cig dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston rgya chen spel /
de nas lo bzhi tsam pe cing du gsang bde 'jigs gsum gyi dbang dang rjes gnang /
khrid lung /
dge bsnyen dang rab byung gi sdom pa 'bogs pa sogs dam pa chos kyi sbyin pa rgya cher bstsal /
dgung grangs nga drug pa me mo glang gi lor /
gong ma'i bka' ltar dza sag dang mnyam du mkhar sngon dang zi ling sogs brgyud dbus lha ldan du phebs /
ta la'i drug pa gnas mchog po ta la'i gser khrir mnga' gsol zhing /
zang zing gi 'bul ba rgya chen bstabs /
paN chen la gong mas gnang ba'i mchod rdzas dang gser dngul phul cing lan lnga mjal /
se 'bras dge gsum gyi dge 'dun rnams la'ang mang 'gyed sogs phul /
de'i phyi lor byang lam brgyud pe cing du log dgung grangs drug  cu re dgu ru phebs pa lcags pho stag gi lor gong mas shing rta ser po dang tham ga rin po che'i rigs dang gos dar sogs gnang sbyin gya nom pa bstsal te rang dgon du log sog yul gyi dgon sde yongs la zhabs kyis bcags te dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi spel /
dgung lo bdun cur phebs pa lcags mo yos kyi lor slar yang pe cing du phebs /
pA dur jIn gyi gzhi ma khang pa bcas nyos te /
no min han gyis mthun rkyen sbyar nas dgon pa nang rten dang bcas pa bzhengs /
chu pho 'brug gi lor /
gong mas dgon pa de la zung gru zi zhes pa'i ming bstsal /
bla ma brgya phrag lhag gis rab gnas bgyis /
dgung lo bdun cu don gsum du phebs pa rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i shing pho rta'i lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes lnga la dgongs pa rdzogs so /

lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje'am ye shes bstan pa'i sgron me ni mdo smad tsong kha byang gi phyogs su rgya bod 'dres mar bsdad pa'i sa cha lang gru'u zhes pa'i 'brog sder /
hor gyi rus su gtogs pa'i yab chi gya tshangs pa gu ru bstan 'dzin dang /
yum bu skyid gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i me mo bya'i lo zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu nyin sku bltams /
dgung lo bzhi par phebs pa na /
'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang pos lcang skya blo bzang chos ldan gyi sprul skur ngos 'dzin mdzad /
skabs der sog po'i wang stobs chen zhig gi bu lcang skya'i sprul sku yin par bsgrags stabs /
re zhig bar gong mar zhu rgyu 'gyangs dgos thug de nas thu'u bkwan chos kyi rgya mtshos thugs khur bzhes te gong mar zhus pas /
gdan sar gdan drongs zhes pa'i bka' thob /
pe cing nas dka' chen shes rab dar rgyas dang dem chi bcas /
lcags byi zla ba lnga par lang gru'u la sprul sku gdan 'dren du 'byor /
tshes gcig nyin par gzim gur du gdan drangs nas gsol ston rgya chen phul zhing /
gong mas gnang ba'i dngos 'bul spam mtho ba phul /
tshes gsum nyin par dgon lung phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur /
tshes pa bcu'i nyin bla dpon ser skya stong phrag mang pos bsu ba dang bcas lcang skya bla brang du 'byor /
lcang skya gong ma'i slob ma a rtse chos rje blo bzang chos 'dzin mdun nas 'bri klog sbyor sdeb sogs sbyong ba'i mgo btsugs /
dgung lo bdun par blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan mdun nas dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i chu mo yos kyi lo la mtsho sngon gyi dpon bstan 'dzin ching wang sogs nas gong mar rgol pa'i dus zing bslangs /
cang jun gung nyen g.yo'u dang /
gung yo'u grung chi gnyis kyis dpung chen btegs nas mtsho sog cham la phab /
dgon sde mang por gong ma'i bka' chad phog shing pho 'brug gi lo  la dgon lung dgon pa shul med du brlags /
lcang skya sprul sku dgon lung nas nyin lam gnyis tsam gyi sar mchod rten thang dgon pa'i nye 'dabs nags tshal stug por brag phug cig tu gab nas bzhugs /
skabs der gong ma yung tring rgyal sar phebs nas lo gnyis pa yin zhing /
lcang skya gong mar zab chos zhus myong bas thugs dad khyad par can yod stabs /
sprul skur bar chad 'byung dogs kyis de 'phral cang jun gnyis la pe cing du gdan drang dgos pa'i bka' phab /
cang jun gnyis kyis thabs sna tshogs la brten te nags tshal nas zi ling du gdan drangs /
de nas rgya nag tu phebs /
gong mas khong zung gru zi dgon par lcang skya gong ma'i gdan sar bkod /
dka' chen shes rab dar rgyas slob dpon du brten nas /
mdo sngags kyi gzhung chen rnams la gsan sbyong mdzad /
dgung lo bco brgyad pa'i dus su rig gnas kun la mkhas par gyur /
rgya dang sog po man ju bcas kyi skad yig kyang khong du chud /

shing pho stag gi lo la gong ma'i bka' bzhin /
rgyal sras bcu bdun pa kheng zi ching wang dang lhan cig tA la'i dbus su gdan drangs nas po ta la'i gdan sar 'god pa'i ched du khams phyogs su phebs /
zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyer gsum nyin mgar thar du 'byor /
tA la'i mdun par gong mas gnang ba'i gser yig bsgrags shing dngos 'bul rgya chen phul /
dgung lo bcu dgu pa shing mo yos kyi lo'i zla ba gsum par khams lho brgyud kyi nyag chu rdzong dang li thang sogs brgyud de dbus su phebs /
zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu bdun nyin par tA la'i po ta lar gdan khrir bkod /
zla ba bcu par gtsang du phebs /
tshes brgyad la bkra shis lhun por 'byor /
tshes dgu nyin par paN chen blo bzang ye shes mjal kha zhus /

mtshan ye shes bstan pa'i sgron me zhes pa gnang /
tshes bcu bdun nyin paN chen mdun nas dge slong gi sdom pa mnos /

'phral du dbus su phyir phebs /
'brug lor rgya nag tu chibs kha bsgyur /
dar mdo sogs brgyud de pe cing du phebs /

zla ba bcu par dbu btsugs /

dgung lo so gsum du phebs pa sa mo sbrul  kyi lor gong mar dgongs pa zhus te mdo smad rang yul du phebs /
tA la'i yon tan rgya mtshos btab pa'i dgon lung du /
khri zur sum pa zhabs drung sogs che dgus ser sbreng dang bcas bsus /
de nas sku 'bum dgon sogs su phebs nas dam chos bstsal /
zla ba brgyad par pe cing du tshur phebs /
khong dgung lo zhe gcig tu phebs pa rab byung bcu gsum pa'i me mo glang gi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes gsum nyin par /

gong mas bka' phebs ltar /
tA la'i skye phreng ngos 'dzin pa'i chad du /
am pan gcig dang gong ma'i bla sman pa gnyis /
dpon chung kha shas dang bcas khams dar rtse mdo sogs brgyud de dbus su phebs /
zla ba bcu gnyis par lha sar 'byor /

de nas thu'u bkwan rgya nag tu phebs nas khong gi slob mar gyur /

pe cing gi bla ma mkhas pa dang /
